周一，斯坦福大学医学院的科学家宣布，他们发明了一种可以将细胞按类型分类的新型诊断工具：一种可打印的微型芯片。这种芯片可以使用标准喷墨打印机制造，每片价格可能在一美分左右。	On Monday, scientists from the Stanford University School of Medicine announced the invention of a new diagnostic tool that can sort cells by type: a tiny printable chip that can be manufactured using standard inkjet printers for possibly about one U.S. cent each.
主要研究人员表示，这可以让低收入国家/地区的患者尽早发现癌症、肺结核、艾滋病和疟疾。在这些国家/地区，乳腺癌等疾病的生存率可能仅为富裕国家的一半。	Lead researchers say this may bring early detection of cancer, tuberculosis, HIV and malaria to patients in low-income countries, where the survival rates for illnesses such as breast cancer can be half those of richer countries.

伊氏西爪龙属于驰龙科，是迅猛龙的表亲。	Hesperonychus elizabethae is a species of the family Dromaeosauridae and is a cousin of Velociraptor .

恒星会散发光和热，这是因为氢原子结合（或聚变）在一起形成更重的元素时产生了能量。	Stars give off light and heat because of the energy made when hydrogen atoms are merged (or fused) together to form heavier elements.

由于表面张力的作用，钢针可以浮在水面上。	The steel needle floats on top of the water because of surface tension.
发生表面张力的原因，是水面的水分子之间互相强烈吸引，它们之间的引力比与水分子与上方空气分子之间的吸引力要大。	Surface tension happens because the water molecules at the surface of the water are strongly attracted to each other more than they are to the air molecules above them.
水分子在水的表面形成了一层看不见的外皮，这层外皮可以让针这样的东西浮在水面上。	The water molecules make an invisible skin on the water’s surface that allows things like the needle to float on top of the water.
现代溜冰鞋的刀刃是双刃的，刃与刃之间有一个凹洞。双刃对冰有更好的抓力（即使是在倾斜的时候）。	The blade on a modern ice skate has a double edge with a concave hollow between them. The two edges allow for a better grasp of the ice, even when tilted.
由于刀片的底部略弯曲，当刀片歪向其中一侧时，与冰接触的刀边弯曲了。	Because the bottom of the blade is slightly curved, as the blade tilts to one side or the other, the edge which is in contact with the ice also curves.
这样一来，溜冰者就可以转弯。冰刀向右倾斜，溜冰者就转向右边。冰刀向左倾斜，溜冰者就转向左边。	This causes the skater to turn. If the skates tilt to the right, the skater turns right, if the skates tilt to the left, the skater turns left.
它们必须消除从光中得到的多余能量。，才能恢复到之前的能量等级。	To return to their previous energy level, they must get rid of the extra energy they got from the light.
它们是通过发射一种被称为“光子”的微小光粒子做到这一点的。	They do this by emitting a tiny particle of light called a "photon".
科学家把这一过程称为“受激辐射”，因为原子受到强光的刺激，引起光子的发射，而光也是辐射的一种。	Scientists call this process "stimulated emission of radiation" because the atoms are stimulated by the bright light, causing the emission of a photon of light, and light is a type of radiation.
下一张图片显示的是原子发射光子的情况。当然，实际上光子要比图片上的样子小得多。	The next picture shows the atoms emitting photons. Of course, in reality photons are a lot smaller than those in the picture.
光子甚至比构成原子的物质还要小！	Photons are even smaller than the stuff that makes up atoms!
使用几百个小时后，灯丝最终被烧坏，而灯泡也不亮了。	After hundreds of hours of operation the filament in the bulb eventually burns out and the light bulb no longer works.
然后需要更换灯泡。更换灯泡时必须小心操作。	The light bulb then needs replacing. It is necessary to be careful in replacing the light bulb.
首先，务必关闭照明灯具的开关或断开电缆连接。	First, the switch for the light fixture needs to be turned off or the cable disconnected.
这是因为，当灯泡还有一部分与插座相连时，当你接触到插座内部或灯泡的金属底座时，电流会流入插座（灯泡金属底座的连接处），让你受到严重的电击。	This is because electricity flowing into the socket where the metallic part of bulb sits can give you a severe electric shock if you touch the inside of the socket or the metal base of the bulb while it is still partly in the socket.
循环系统的主要器官是心脏，心脏负责输送血液。	The major organ of the circulatory system is the heart, which pumps the blood.
血液通过被称为动脉的管道从心脏流出，然后通过称为静脉的管道回流到心脏。最小的管道叫做毛细血管。	Blood goes away from the heart in tubes called arteries and comes back to the heart in tubes called veins. The smallest tubes are called capillaries.
三角龙的牙齿不仅能咬碎树叶，还能咬碎非常坚硬的树枝和树根。	A triceratops' teeth would have been able to crush not only leaves but even very tough branches and roots.
一些科学家认为，三角龙以苏铁为食，苏铁是白垩纪时期很常见的一种植物。	Some scientists think Triceratops ate cycads, which are a type of plant that was common in the Cretaceous.
这些植物看起来像一棵小棕榈树，树冠由钉子般的锋利叶子组成。	These plants look like a small palm tree with a crown of sharp, spiky leaves.
在吃树干之前，三角龙会用它强有力的喙嘴剥去树叶。	A Triceratops could have used its strong beak to strip off the leaves before eating the trunk.
其他科学家认为这些植物有毒，所以恐龙不太可能吃它们，即便现在树懒和其他动物例如鹦鹉（恐龙的后代）可以吃有毒的叶子或水果。	Other scientists argue that these plants are very poisonous so it is unlikely that any dinosaur ate them, even though today the sloth and other animals like the parrot (a descendant of the dinosaurs) can eat poisonous leaves or fruit.
木卫一的重力会对我产生怎样的作用力？如果你站在木卫一表面，你的体重会比在地球上轻。	How would Io's gravity pull on me? If you stood on the surface of Io, you would weigh less than you do on Earth.
一个在地球上重 200 磅（90公斤）的人，在木卫一上的重量约为 36 磅（16公斤）。因此重力理所当然地对你产生了较小的牵引力。	A person who weighs 200 pounds (90kg) on Earth would weigh about 36 pounds (16kg) on Io. So the gravity, of course, pulls less on you.
太阳并没有像地球那样可以站在上面的地壳。整个太阳是由气体、火和等离子体组成的。	The Sun doesn't have a crust like the Earth that you can stand on. The whole Sun is made out of gases, fire, and plasma.
当你距离太阳中心越远，气体就越稀薄。	The gas becomes thinner as you go farther from the center of the Sun.
我们看到的太阳外部称作光球层，意即“光之球”。	The outer-part we see when we look at the Sun is called the photosphere, which means "ball of light".
约三千年后，也就是在1610年，意大利的天文学家伽利略·伽利莱（Galileo Galilei）使用望远镜观测天体，发现金星具有着与月球一致的相位。	About three thousand years later, in 1610, Italian astronomer Galileo Galilei used a telescope to observe that Venus has phases, just as the moon does.
相变的发生是因为金星（或月球）只有面向太阳的一边被照到。金星的相变支持了哥白尼的理论，即行星围绕太阳旋转。	Phases happen because only the side of Venus (or of the Moon) facing the Sun is lighted. The phases of Venus supported the theory of Copernicus that the planets go around the Sun.
然后，几年后的 1639 年，一位名叫耶利米·霍罗克斯 (Jeremiah Horrocks) 的英国天文学家观测到了一次金星凌日。	Then, a few years later in 1639, an English astronomer named Jeremiah Horrocks observed a transit of Venus.
重新征服丹麦法区域 (Danelaw) 后，英格兰经历了很长的和平时期。	England had experienced a long period of peace after the reconquest of the Danelaw.
然而，在 991 年，埃塞尔雷德面对的是一个世纪前的古斯鲁姆舰队之后最大的维京舰队。	However in 991 Ethelred was faced with a Viking fleet larger than any since Guthrum's a century earlier.
这支舰队由奥拉夫·特里格瓦松率领。他是挪威人，志在将挪威从丹麦手中夺回来。	This fleet was led by Olaf Trygvasson, a Norwegian with ambitions to reclaim his country from Danish domination.
在初期军事失利之后，埃塞尔雷德终于与奥拉夫达成协议，奥拉夫重返挪威试图夺回王位，但算不上成功。	After initial military setbacks, Ethelred was able to agree to terms with Olaf, who returned to Norway to try to gain his kingdom with mixed success.
韩文字母是唯一一个特意发明供日常使用的字母表，是于 1444 年世宗皇帝（1418 - 1450）统治时期所发明的。	Hangeul is the only purposely invented alphabet in popular daily use. The alphabet was invented in 1444 during the reign of King Sejong (1418 – 1450).
世宗大王为朝鲜王朝的第四任君主，也是最受推崇的君主之一。	King Sejong was the fourth king of the Joseon Dynasty and is one of the most highly regarded.
他最初将韩语字母发音表命名为“训民正音”，意思是“用于教导人民的正确发音”。	He originally named the Hangeul alphabet Hunmin Jeongeum, which means "the correct sounds for the instruction of the people".
关于梵语的起源有很多说法。其中之一是雅利安人从西方移民到印度，将自己的语言带到这里。	There are many theories to how Sanskrit came into existence. One of them is about an Aryan migration from the west into India who brought their language with them.
梵语是一种古老的语言，能与欧洲的拉丁语相媲美。	Sanskrit is an ancient language and is comparable to the Latin language spoken in Europe.
世界上已知最早的书是用梵文写的。《奥义书》编撰完成后，梵文由于等级制度的原因逐渐消失。	The earliest known book in the world was written in Sanskrit. After the compilation of Upanishads, Sanskrit just faded due to hierarchy.
梵语是一种博大精深的语言，也是许多现代印度语的起源，就像拉丁语是法语和西班牙语等欧洲语言的起源一样。	Sanskrit is a very complex and rich language, which has served to be the source for many modern Indian languages, just like Latin is the source for European languages like French and Spanish.
对法作战结束后，德国又开始为入侵不列颠岛做准备。	With the battle for France over, Germany began to get ready to invade the island of Britain.
德国将此次袭击的代号定为“海狮行动”。英国军队从敦刻尔克撤退时失去了大部分重型武器和补给，元气大伤。	Germany code-named the attack “Operation Sealion”. Most of the British Army's heavy weapons and supplies had been lost when it evacuated from Dunkirk, so the army was fairly weak.
但皇家海军还是比德国海军（“Kriegsmarine”）强得多，可以摧毁任何跨越英吉利海峡的入侵舰队。	But the Royal Navy was still much stronger than the German Navy (“Kriegsmarine”) and could have destroyed any invasion fleet sent across the English Channel.
然而，很少有皇家海军舰艇在潜在的入侵路线附近驻扎，因为海军将领们担心舰艇会被德国的空袭击沉。	However, very few Royal Navy ships were based near the likely invasion routes as the admirals were afraid they would be sunk by German air attack.
让我们先来解释一下意大利的计划。意大利基本上属于德国和日本的“小兄弟”。	Let's start with an explanation about Italy's plans. Italy was mainly the "little brother" of Germany and Japan.
该国陆军和海军都比较弱，尽管他们在战争开始前不久建造了四艘新舰船。	It had a weaker army and a weaker navy, although they had just built four new ships right before the beginning of the war.
意大利的主要目标是非洲国家。为了夺取这些国家，他们需要一个军队基地，以便军队可以驶穿地中海，入侵非洲。	Italy's main goals were African countries. To capture those countries, they would need to have a troop launching pad, so as troops could sail across the Mediterranean Sea and invade Africa.
为此，他们不得不将英国在埃及的基地和船舰撤出。除了采取这些行动，意大利的战舰本不应该有所行动。	For that, they had to get rid of British bases and ships in Egypt. Besides those actions, Italy's battleships were not supposed to do anything else.
现在来看日本。和英国一样，日本是一个岛国。	Now for Japan. Japan was an island country, just like Britain.
潜水艇是为了在水底下行驶而设计的船，而且潜水艇在水面下停留的时间较长。	Submarines are ships designed to travel underwater, and remain there for an extended amount of time.
第一次世界大战和第二次世界大战期间都使用了潜水艇。 那时它们的速度很慢，射击范围也非常有限。	Submarines were used in World War I and World War II. Back then they were very slow and had a very limited shooting range.
在战争开始时，它们大多在海面上航行，但随着雷达的发展和精确度的提高，潜艇被迫潜入水下以免被发现。	In the beginning of the war they mostly travelled on top of the sea, but as radar began developing and becoming more accurate the submarines were forced to go under water to avoid being seen.
德国潜艇被称为 U 型潜艇。德国人非常擅长导航和操作潜艇。	German submarines were called U-Boats. The Germans were very good at navigating and operating their submarines.
由于德国人在潜艇方面很成功，他们在战后不获托管大量潜艇。	Because of their success with submarines, after the war Germans aren't trusted to have many of them.
是的！图坦卡蒙国王，有时也被称为“图特王”或“少年国王”，他是现代最著名的古埃及国王之一。	Yes! King Tutankhamun, sometimes referred to as "King Tut" or "The Boy King", is one of the most well known ancient Egyptian kings in modern times.
有趣的是，他在古代并不被认为是举足轻重的人物，而且不被记录于大多数古代国王的名单。	Interestingly, he was not considered to be very important in ancient times and was not recorded on most ancient king lists.
然而，1922 年发现了他的墓穴，让他成了名人。虽然有许多过去的坟墓被盗，但这座坟墓几乎未遭破坏。	However, the discovery of his tomb in 1922 made him a celebrity. While many tombs of the past were robbed, this tomb was left virtually undisturbed.
图坦卡蒙的大部分陪葬品都保存完好，其中包括数千件由贵金属和稀有宝石制成的文物。	Most of the items buried with Tutankhamun have been well preserved, including thousands of artefacts made from precious metals and rare stones.
辐轮的发明使亚述人的战车更轻便、更迅速，行驶起来可以更轻松地超过士兵和其他战车。	The invention of spoke wheels made Assyrian chariots lighter, faster, and better prepared to outrun soldiers and other chariots.
他们从致命的十字弓中射出的利箭，能穿透敌军的盔甲。公元前 1000 年前后，亚述人使用了第一批骑兵。	Arrows from their deadly crossbows could penetrate the armor of rival soldiers. About 1000 B.C., the Assyrians introduced the first cavalry.
骑兵是指在马背上作战的军队。当时尚未发明马鞍，因此亚述骑兵只能骑在光秃秃的马背上作战。	A cavalry is an army that fights on horseback. The saddle had not yet been invented, so the Assyrian cavalry fought on the bare backs of their horses.
我们知道许多希腊政治家、科学家和艺术家。希腊文化中最有名的人可能是有着传奇色彩的盲人诗人荷马。他创作了希腊文学的两部杰作：《伊利亚特》和《奥德赛》。	We know many Greek politicians, scientists, and artists. Possibly the most known person of this culture is Homer, the legendary blind poet, who composed two masterpieces of Greek literature: the poems Iliad and Odyssey.
索福克勒斯（Sophocles ）和阿里斯托芬（Aristophanes）仍然是受欢迎的剧作家，他们的戏剧被认为是世界文学中最伟大的作品之一。	Sophocles and Aristophanes are still popular playwrights and their plays are considered to be among the greatest works of world literature.
另一个著名的希腊人是数学家毕达哥拉斯，他最有名的成就是提出了关于直角三角形各边关系的著名定理。	Another famous Greek is a mathematician Pythagoras, mostly known for his famous theorem about relations of the sides of right triangles.
对于说印地语的人口数，有不同的说法。据估计，印地语是世界上第二到第四最常用的语言。	There are varying estimates for how many people speak Hindi. It is estimated to be between the second and fourth most commonly spoken language in the world.
母语人数取决于紧密相关的方言是否计算在内。	The number of native speakers varies depending on whether or not very closely related dialects are counted.
据估计，会说这种语言的人数量范围在 3.4 亿到 5 亿之间，而能听懂这种语言的人则多达 8 亿。	Estimates range from 340 million to 500 million speakers, and as many as 800 million people can understand the language.
印度语和乌尔都语有着相似的词汇，但文字的书写方式不同；在日常对话中，这两种语言通常可以交流互通。	Hindi and Urdu are similar in vocabulary but different in script; in everyday conversations, speakers of both languages can usually understand each other.
15 世纪前后，爱沙尼亚北部深受德国文化的影响。	Around the 15th century, northern Estonia was under great cultural influence of Germany.
一些德国修道士想让上帝更接近本国人，所以他们发明了爱沙尼亚文字语言。	Some German monks wanted to bring God closer to the native people, so they invented the Estonian literal language.
它是在德语字母表中加了一个字母“Õ/õ”。	It was based on the German alphabet and one character "Õ/õ" was added.
随着时间的推移，许多德语外来词与原有词汇合并。这就是启蒙运动的开始。	As time passed, many words that were borrowed from German coalesced. This was the beginning of enlightenment.
传统上，王位继承人在完成学业后会直接入伍。	Traditionally, the heir to the throne would go straight into the military after finishing school.

土耳其位于欧洲的部分（地处巴尔干半岛的东色雷斯或鲁米利亚）占其国土面积的 3％。	European Turkey (eastern Thrace or Rumelia in the Balkan peninsula) includes 3% of the country.
土耳其领土长 1,600 多公里（1,000 英里），宽 800 公里（500 英里），大致呈矩形。	The territory of Turkey is more than 1,600 kilometres (1,000 mi) long and 800 km (500 mi) wide, with a roughly rectangular shape.
土耳其的国土面积（包括湖泊）为 783,562 平方公里（300,948 平方英里），其中 755,688 平方公里（291,773 平方英里）位于西南亚，23,764 平方公里（9,174 平方英里）位于欧洲。	Turkey's area, including lakes, occupies 783,562 square kilometres (300,948 sq mi), of which 755,688 square kilometres (291,773 sq mi) are in south west Asia and 23,764 square kilometres (9,174 sq mi) in Europe.
土耳其的面积在世界上排第 37 位，大约是法国本土和英国面积的总和。	Turkey's area makes it the world's 37th-largest country, and is about the size of Metropolitan France and the United Kingdom combined.

今天的比利时有部分地区过去属于卢森堡，但在 19 世纪 30 年代的比利时革命后被划入比利时。	Present-day parts of Belgium were part of Luxembourg in the past but became Belgian after the 1830s Belgian Revolution.

火灾过后，堡垒得到维护和保护，成为不丹最备受瞩目的景点之一。	After the fire, the fortress was preserved and protected, remaining to be one of Bhutan's most sensational attractions.

交互设计要求你重新评估有关媒体制作的假设，并学会非线性思考。	Interactive design requires that you re-assess your assumptions about media production and learn to think in a non-linear ways.
交互设计要求项目的各个组成部分相互联系，但也可以作为一个独立实体存在。	Interactive design requires that components of a project connect to each other, but also make sense as a separate entity.
变焦镜头的缺点是，要想实现一定的焦距范围，所需的焦距复杂度和透镜元件的数量远远大于定焦镜头。	The disadvantage of zoom lenses is that the focal complexity and number of lens elements required to achieve a range of focal lengths is much greater than for prime lenses.
随着镜头制造商在镜头生产方面达到更高的标准，这已经不算什么问题了。	This is becoming less of an issue as lens manufacturers achieve higher standards in lens production.
这使得变焦镜头可以拍出与固定焦距镜头质量相媲美的照片。	This has allowed zoom lenses to produce pictures of a quality comparable to that achieved by lenses with fixed focal length.

大多数电视节目都是为娱乐大众而制作的。	Most televisions are made in a way to please the general public.
出于该原因，你在电视上看到的画面边框，包括顶部、底部和侧边，都被裁剪了。	For that reason, everything you see on the TV had the borders cut, top, bottom and sides.
这样做是为了保证图像能覆盖住整个屏幕。这叫做“过度扫描”。	This is made to ensure that the image covers the whole screen. That is called overscan.
遗憾的是，当你制作 DVD 时，它的边框很可能也会被裁剪掉，而且如果视频中的字幕太靠近底部，那么字幕也会显示不完整。	Unfortunately, when you make a DVD, it's borders will most likely be cut too, and if the video had subtitles too close to the bottom, they won't be fully shown.

人们即使站在千年的废墟中，也很容易回想起早已逝去的战争的声音和气味，几乎能听到鹅卵石上马蹄的碰撞声，也能闻到从地牢坑里冒出来的恐惧气息。	Even standing amidst thousand year-old ruins it is easy to bring to mind the sounds and smells of battles long gone, to almost hear the clatter of hooves on the cobbles and to smell the fear rising from the dungeon pits.

权力的平衡是欧洲国家寻求维护全体欧洲国家国家主权的制度。	The balance of power was a system in which European nations sought to maintain the national sovereignty of all European states.
这种理念是，所有欧洲国家必须设法阻止某个国家/地区独自变得强大，因此，各国政府为了保持平衡经常更换盟友。	The concept was that all European nations had to seek to prevent one nation from becoming powerful, and thus national governments often changed their alliances in order to maintain the balance.
西班牙继承权之战标志着第一场以权力平衡为核心问题的战争。	The War of Spanish Succession marked the first war whose central issue was the balance of power.
这标志着一个重要的变化，因为欧洲大国将无法再以宗教战争为借口。因此，三十年战争将是最后一场被贴上宗教战争标签的战争。	This marked an important change, as European powers would no longer have the pretext of being religious wars. Thus, the Thirty Years' War would be the last war to be labeled a religious war.
公元前 356 年 7 月 21 日，赫洛斯塔图斯 (Herostratus) 的纵火行为导致位于以弗所 (Ephesus) 的阿尔忒弥斯神庙毁于一旦。	The temple of Artemis at Ephesus was destroyed on July 21, 356 BCE in an act of arson committed by Herostratus.
据故事情节所写，此人愿不惜一切代价出人头地。愤慨的以弗所人宣布黑若斯达特斯（Herostratus）之名罄竹难书。	According to the story, his motivation was fame at any cost. The Ephesians, outraged, announced that Herostratus' name never be recorded.
希腊历史学家斯特拉博 (Strabo) 后来提到了这个名字，也就是我们今天所熟知的名字。圣殿在亚历山大大帝出生的当晚被毁。	The Greek historian Strabo later noted the name, which is how we know today. The temple was destroyed on the same night that Alexander the Great was born.
亚历山大大帝原本提议重建这座神庙，但其提案遭到拒绝。随后，在亚历山大死后，该神庙于公元前 323 年得以重建。	Alexander, as king, offered to pay to rebuild the temple, but his offer was denied. Later, after Alexander died, the temple was rebuilt in 323 BCE.
确保你的手尽可能地放松，同时仍可以正确地敲击所有的音符—手指也尽量不要做太多无关的动作。	Make sure your hand is as relaxed as possible while still hitting all the notes correctly - also try not to make much extraneous motion with your fingers.
这样就能让你尽可能节省体力。记住，不用像在钢琴上那样用力敲击琴键来提升音量。	This way, you will tire yourself out as little as possible. Remember there's no need to hit the keys with a lot of force for extra volume like on the piano.
为了提高手风琴的音量，可以更用力或以更快的速度拉风箱。	On the accordion, to get extra volume, you use the bellows with more pressure or speed.
神秘主义追求与终极现实、神性、精神真理或上帝进行交流、认同或达成知觉意识。	Mysticism is the pursuit of communion with, identity with, or conscious awareness of an ultimate reality, divinity, spiritual truth, or God.
信徒们寻求一种对神圣的现实/神性或诸神的直接体验、直觉或者顿悟。	The believer seeks a direct experience, intuition, or insight into divine reality/the deity or dieties.
追随者追求某种生活方式或旨在滋养这些经验的修行。	Followers pursue certain ways of living, or practices that are intended to nurture those experiences.
神秘主义可以与其他形式的宗教信仰和崇拜区分开来，因为它强调对独特意识状态的个人直接体验，特别是那些和平的、有洞察力的、幸福的、甚至是狂喜的意识状态。	Mysticism can be distinguished from other forms of religious belief and worship by its emphasis on the direct personal experience of a unique state of consciousness, particularly those of a peaceful, insightful, blissful, or even ecstatic character.
锡克教是来自印度次大陆的一种宗教。它在 15 世纪起源于旁遮普地区，来自印度教传统的内部宗派分裂。	Sikhism is a religion from the Indian sub-continent. It originated in the Punjab region during the 15th century from a sectarian split within the Hindu tradition.
锡克教徒认为，他们信仰的是与印度教不同的一种宗教，尽管他们承认锡克教源自印度教，也包含印度教的传统。	Sikhs consider their faith to be a separate religion from Hinduism though they acknowledge its Hindu roots and traditions.
锡克教徒把自己的宗教称为 Gurmat，在旁遮普语中是“古鲁（导师）之路”的意思。古鲁是所有印度宗教的基本组成部分，但在锡克教中地位特别高，成为了锡克教信仰的核心。	Sikhs call their religion Gurmat, which is Punjabi for "way of the guru". The guru is a fundamental aspect of all Indian religions but in Sikhism has taken on an importance that forms the core of Sikh beliefs.
该宗教于 15 世纪由古鲁·纳纳克 (1469-1539) 创立。随后又有九位古鲁。	The religion was founded in the 15th century by Guru Nanak (1469–1539). There followed in succession a further nine gurus.
然而，在 1956 年 6 月，当波兰工人抗议食品短缺和减薪的骚乱演变成对共产主义制度本身的抗议时，赫鲁晓夫的承诺面临着考验。	However, in June 1956, Krushchev's promises were put to the test when riots in Poland, where workers were protesting against food shortages and wage cuts, turned into a general protest against Communism.
尽管在最后，赫鲁晓夫派出坦克恢复了秩序，但他还是对一些经济要求做出了让步，并同意任命受民众欢迎的瓦迪斯瓦夫·哥穆尔卡 (Wladyslaw Gomulka) 为新总理。	Although in the end, Krushchev sent in tanks to restore order, he did give way to some economic demands and agreed to appoint the popular Wladyslaw Gomulka as the new prime minister.
印度河流域文明是青铜时代的文明，位于印度西北部次大陆，覆盖的区域包括了现代巴基斯坦的大部分地区，以及印度西北部和阿富汗东北部的一些地区。	The Indus Valley Civilization was a Bronze Age civilisation in the northwest Indian subcontinent encompassing most of modern-day Pakistan and some regions in northwest India and northeast Afghanistan.
印度河盆地的文明发展繁荣，该文明因此得名。	The civilisation flourished in the basins of the Indus River wherefore it derives its name.
尽管一些学者推测，鉴于这一文明也存在于如今已然干涸的萨拉斯瓦蒂河流域，将该文明称为“印度河-萨拉斯瓦蒂河文明”才算恰如其分，不过一些人称其为“哈拉帕文明”——得名于20世纪20年代在该区域发掘的第一个遗址“哈拉帕”。	Although some scholars speculate that since the civilisation also existed in the basins of the now dried up Sarasvati River, it should be aptly called the Indus-Sarasvati Civilization, while some call it the Harappan Civilization after Harappa, the first of its sites to be excavated in the 1920s.
罗马帝国的军国主义性质促进了医学的进步和发展。	The militaristic nature of the Roman empire aided in the development of medical advances.
奥古斯都皇帝开始招募医生，甚至组建了第一支罗马医疗队，用于战后医疗。	Doctors began to be recruited by Emperor Augustus and even formed the first Roman Medical Corps for use in the aftermath of battles.
外科医生对各种镇静剂都有了解，包括从罂粟种子中提取的吗啡和从莨菪种子中提取的东莨菪碱。	Surgeons had knowledge of various sedatives including morphine from extracts of poppy seeds and scopolamine from herbane seeds.
除了用止血带和动脉钳来阻止血液流动外，他们已能熟练通过截肢来挽救坏疽患者。	They became proficient at amputation to save patients from gangrene as well as tourniquets and arterial clamps to stem blood flow.
在几个世纪里，罗马帝国在医学领域取得了巨大成果，构成了我们今天所知晓的大部分知识。	Over multiple centuries, the Roman empire led to great gains in the field of medicine and formed much of the knowledge we know today.
净土折纸，其限制规则是一次只能进行一次折叠，不允许反向折叠这样更复杂的动作，并且所有折叠的位置都必须简单明了。	Pureland origami is origami with the restriction that only one fold may be done at a time, more complex folds like reverse folds are not allowed, and all folds have straightforward locations.
它是由约翰•史密斯 (John Smith) 在 20 世纪 70 年代研发的，用于帮助缺乏经验的折纸人或动手能力差的人。	It was developed by John Smith in the 1970s to help inexperienced folders or those with limited motor skills.
孩子还小的时候，就能意识到种族和种族刻板印象，这些种族刻板印象会影响其行为。	Children develop an awareness of race and racial stereotypes quite young and these racial stereotypes affect behavior.
例如，如果人们模式化地认为某个少数族裔的孩子在学校表现不好，那么这些孩子一旦了解了关于自己族裔的模式化观念，他们在学校往往就有不好的表现。	For instance, children who identify with a racial minority that is stereotyped as not doing well in school tend to not do well in school once they learn about the stereotype associated with their race.
MySpace 是美国第三大最受欢迎的网站，目前有 5,400 万个注册帐号。	MySpace is the third most popular website used in the United States and has 54 million profiles currently.
这些网站得到了很多关注，尤其是在教育领域。	These websites have gotten a lot of attention, especially in the education setting.
这些网站也有好处，比如可以轻松创建一个包含博客、视频、照片等内容的班级页面。	There are positive aspects to these websites, which include, being able to easily setup a class page which can include blogs, videos, photos, and other features.
只需提供一个网址，就能轻松访问该页面。这对不会用键盘或拼写有困难的学生来说，更加容易记住，输入也更简单。	This page can easily be accessed by providing just one web address, which makes it easy to remember and easy to type in for students who may have trouble using the keyboard or with spelling.
它可以进行个性化设置以便阅读，也可根据需求使用或多或少的颜色。	It can be customized to make it easy to read and also with as much or little color as desired.
“注意力缺失症“是一种神经系统综合症，三种典型的限定症状包括冲动、注意力分散、多动或精力过剩。	Attention Deficit Disorder "is a neurological syndrome whose classic defining triad of symptoms including impulsivity, distractibility, and hyperactivity or excess energy".
这不是学习能力缺失，而是学习障碍；这“影响着全美儿童的 3% 到 5%，人数可能多达 200 万”。	It is not a learning disability, it is a learning disorder; it "affects 3 to 5 percent of all children, perhaps as many as 2 million American children".
患有多动症的孩子很难专心做事，例如做作业，但他们能够集中精力做自己喜欢的事情，比如玩游戏，看喜欢的卡通片，或者写一些不加标点符号的句子。	Children with ADD have a hard time focusing on things like school work, but they can concentrate on things they enjoy doing like playing games or watching their favorite cartoons or writing sentences without punctuation.
这些孩子往往会陷入很多麻烦。因为正常的方法无法刺激他们的大脑，为了刺激大脑，他们“做出危险行为、打架、挑战权威”。	These children tend to get into a lot of trouble, because they "engage in risky behaviors, get into fights, and challenge authority" in order to stimulate their brain, since their brain can not be stimulated by normal methods.
注意力缺陷障碍（ADD）会影响患病孩童与其同龄人的关系，因为其他儿童无法理解患者做出行为、进行拼写的原因所在，也不理解为什么他们的成熟程度与众不同。	ADD affects relationships with other peers because other children can not understand why they act the way that they do or why they spell they way they do or that their maturity level is different.
当获取知识和进行学习的能力发生如上所述的变化时，获取知识的基本速率也相应地产生变化。	As the ability to obtain knowledge and to learn changed in such a way as mentioned above the base rate at which knowledge was obtained changed.
获取信息的方法不尽相同。压力不再存在于个人回忆中，但回忆文本的能力变得更加重要。	The approach to obtaining information was different. No longer did pressure reside within individual recall, but the ability to recall text became more of a focus.
文艺复兴从根本上让学习和知识传播的方式产生了重大变化。	In essence, the Renaissance made a significant change in the approach to learning and the dissemination of knowledge.
原始人类与其他灵长类动物不同的地方在于，他们不再用双手移动身体、托起重物、在树林里荡来荡去。	Unlike other primates, hominids no longer use their hands in locomotion or bearing weight or swinging through the trees.
黑猩猩手脚的大小和长度相似，这反映出手在指背行走中用来承重的事实。	The chimpanzee's hand and foot are similar in size and length, reflecting the hand's use for bearing weight in knuckle walking.
人类的手比脚短，指（趾）骨更直。	The human hand is shorter than the foot, with straighter phalanges.
200 万到 300 万年前的手骨化石，都无不体现出手部特征，从移动方式到操作方式，经历了改变。	Fossil hand bones two million to three million years old reveal this shift in specialization of the hand from locomotion to manipulation.
有些人认为，经常做人工诱导、清晰的梦会让人精疲力竭。	Some people believe that experiencing many artificially induced lucid dreams often enough can be very exhausting.
造成这种现象的主要原因是清晰的梦境延长了快速眼动状态之间的时间间隔。	The main reason for this phenomenon is the result of the lucid dreams expanding the length of time between REM states.
每晚快速眼动期 (REM) 越短，在这种状态下睡个好觉、恢复元气的频率就越少，身体可能会出问题。	With fewer REMs per night, this state in which you experience actual sleep and your body recovers becomes infrequent enough to become a problem.
这就像每隔二三十分钟就醒来看电视那样令人筋疲力竭。	This is just as exhausting as if you were to wake up every twenty or thirty minutes and watch TV.
其效果取决于你的大脑每晚做清醒梦的频率。	The effect is dependent on how often your brain attempts to lucidly dream per night.

也许最常见的旅游类型，也是大多数人一想到旅游就会想到的：休闲旅游。	Perhaps the most common type of tourism is what most people associate with traveling: Recreation tourism.

保持健康的能量平衡，坚持有效补充水分的习惯，了解合理使用营养补品的各个方面，能够帮助运动员们改善表现，增加运动乐趣。	Maintaining a healthy energy balance, practicing effective hydration habits, and understanding the various aspects of supplementation practices can help athletes improve their performance and increase their enjoyment of the sport.

原子可被视为是全部物质的基本组成模块之一。	The atom can be considered to be one of the fundamental building blocks of all matter.
根据简化的波尔模型显示，这是一个非常复杂的实体，包含了一个由电子环绕的中心原子核，这些电子有点像绕着太阳运行的行星。详见图 1.1。	Its a very complex entity which consists, according to a simplified Bohr model, of a central nucleus orbited by electrons, somewhat similar to planets orbiting the sun - see Figure 1.1.

靠近受害者时，需要注意其姿势和任何无意识的危险信号。	You need to notice the victim's position as you approach him or her and any automatic red flags.
如果你想帮助别人时受伤，你只会使事情变得更糟。	If you get hurt trying to help, you may only serve to make matters worse.
研究发现，抑郁、恐惧以及把病情灾难化的情绪，在腰疼患者的疼痛和残疾中起到了中介作用。	The study found that depression, fear and catastrophising mediated the relationship between pain and disability in lower back pain sufferers.
只有杞人忧天思维的影响，而不是沮丧和恐惧的影响，才能有条件地每周定期进行结构性体育锻炼。	Only the effects of catastrophizing, not depression and fear was conditional of regular weekly structured PA sessions.
参与定期训练的人在对疼痛的被动感知方面需要更多支持，以帮助他们区分慢性疼痛和不适感与正常身体运动的区别。	Those participating in regular activity required more support in terms of negative perception of pain distinguishing the differences of chronic pain and discomfort feel from normal physical movement.
视觉或看的能力依赖于视觉系统的感觉器官，即眼睛。	Vision, or the ability to see depends on visual system sensory organs or eyes.
眼睛的构造有许多种，其复杂程度取决于生物体的需要。	There are many different constructions of eyes, ranging in complexity depending on the requirements of the organism.
不同的构造有不同的功能，对不同的波长敏感，且敏锐度不同。它们也需要不同的处理方式来理解输入，并需要不同数量的输入才能达到最佳效果。	The different constructions have different capabilities, are sensitive to different wave-lengths and have differing degrees of acuity, also they require different processing to make sense of the input and different numbers to work optimally.
种群是指在特定地理区域内特定种类生物体的集合。	A population is the collection of organisms of a particular species within a given geographic area.
当种群中的所有个体在某一特定表型性状上完全相同时，就称之为单型。	When all individuals in a population are identical with regard to a particular phenotypic trait they are known as monomorphic.
当个体表现出某一性状的几个变体时，它们就是多态的。	When the individuals show several variants of a particular trait they are polymorphic.
行军蚁群的行进和筑巢也分不同的阶段。	Army ant colonies march and nest in different phases as well.
在迁徙阶段，行军蚁在夜间出行，白天停下来安营。	In the nomadic phase, army ants march at night and stop to camp during the day.
当可利用的食物减少时，这个蚁群就会迎来迁徙期。在这一阶段，蚁群会建造每天更换的临时巢穴。	The colony begins a nomadic phase when available food has decreased. During this phase, the colony makes temporary nests that are changed everyday.
这种游牧性的横冲直撞行为每次都会持续 17 天左右。	Each of these nomadic rampages or marches lasts for approximately 17 days.
什么是细胞？“细胞”一词来源于拉丁语“cella”，意思是“小房间”，最初是由观察软木结构的显微镜学家创造的。	What is a cell? The word cell comes from the Latin word "cella", meaning "small room", and it was first coined by a microscopist observing the structure of cork.
细胞是所有生物的基本构成单位，所有生物体都是由一个或多个细胞构成的。	The cell is the basic unit of all living things, and all organisms are composed of one or more cells.
实际上，细胞在生物研究中有着如此基础和关键的地位，以至于它们常被称为“生命的基本单位”。	Cells are so basic and critical to the study of life, in fact, that they are often referred to as "the building blocks of life".
神经系统通过向全身发送神经脉冲来保持血液流动顺畅，从而维持体内平衡。	The Nervous System maintains homeostasis by sending nerve impulses through out the body to keep the flow of blood going as well as undisturbed.
这些神经脉冲可以非常迅速地传送到全身，让身体免受任何潜在威胁的伤害。	These nerve impulses can be sent so quickly throughout the body which helps keep the body safe from any potential threat.
与其他猛烈的风暴相比，龙卷风袭击的区域较小，但可以摧毁途经的一切。	Tornadoes strike a small area compared to other violent storms, but they can destroy everything in their path.
龙卷风能将树木连根拔起，将建筑物上的木板撕下，把汽车抛向天空。龙卷风中的百分之二最为猛烈，能持续肆虐三小时以上。	Tornadoes uproot trees, rip boards from buildings, and fling cars up into the sky. The most violent two percent of tornadoes last more than three hours.
这些怪物般的风暴，风速高达每小时 480 公里（133 m/s; 300 mph）。	These monster storms have winds up to 480 km/h (133 m/s; 300 mph).
几千年来，人类一直在制作和使用放大镜。	Humans have been making and using lenses for magnification for thousands and thousands of years.
然而，第一个真正的望远镜是 16 世纪晚期在欧洲制造的。	However, the first true telescopes were made in Europe in the late 16th century.
这些望远镜使用了两个透镜的组合，使远处的物体看起来既近又大。	These telescopes used a combination of two lenses to make distant objects appear both nearer and larger.
贪婪和自私永远与我们同在，合作的本质就是当大多数人受益时，短期的自私行为总能带来更多利益	Greed and selfishness will always be with us and it is the nature of cooperation that when the majority benefit there will always be more to gain in the short term by acting selfishly
希望大多数人都能意识到，从长远来看，与他人合作才是最佳选择。	Hopefully, most people will realise that their long term best option is to work together with others.
许多人梦想着人类有一天可以移民到其他星球，探索其他世界。有些人想知道宇宙有什么；有些人相信其他行星上可能有外星人或其他生命。	Many people dream of the day when humans can travel to another star and explore other worlds, some people wonder what's out there some belive that aliens or other life may live on another plant.
但如果这种情况真的发生了，那么它很可能在很长一段时间内都不会再发生了。这些恒星非常分散，“相邻”的恒星相隔数万亿英里。	But, if this ever does happen probably won't happen for a very long time. The stars are so spread out that there are trillions of miles between stars that are "neighbors".
也许有一天，你的子孙后代会生活在外星世界，猜测着他们远古的祖先当时过得是怎样的一种生活。	Maybe one day, your great grandchildren will be standing atop an alien world wondering about their ancient ancestors?
动物由许多细胞组成。动物吃了食物后会在体内将其消化。大部分动物都能移动。	Animals are made of many cells. They eat things and digest them inside. Most animals can move.
只有动物有脑（但也不是所有动物都有，比如水母就没有脑）。	Only animals have brains (though not even all animals do; jellyfish, for example, do not have brains).
地球上的各个角落都有动物的身影。它们有的在地下挖洞，有的在海洋中畅游，有的在天空中翱翔。	Animals are found all over the earth. They dig in the ground, swim in the oceans, and fly in the sky.
细胞是各类生物体中最小的结构和功能单位。	A cell is the smallest structural and functional unit of a living (things) organism.
Cell（细胞）一词源自拉丁语cella（意思是小房间）。	Cell comes from the Latin word cella which means small room.
在显微镜下观察生物，你会发现它们是由小方块或小球组成的。	If you look at living things under a microscope, you will see that they are made of small squares or balls.
来自英国的生物学家罗伯特·胡克 (Robert Hooke) 用显微镜看到了软木塞中藏有一些小方块。	Robert Hooke, a biologist from England, saw small squares in cork with a microscope.
它们看上去像房间。他是第一个观察死亡细胞的人	They looked like rooms. He was the first person to observe dead cells
元素和化合物可以在发生化学变化的情况下改变物态。	Elements and compounds can move from one state to another and not change.
气态氮仍具有与液态氮相同的性质。液态氮的密度更大，但是分子还是一样的。	Nitrogen as a gas still has the same properties as liquid nitrogen. The liquid state is denser but the molecules are still the same.
另一个例子是水。化合物水是由两个氢原子和一个氧原子组成的。	Water is another example. The compound water is made up of two hydrogen atoms and one oxygen atom.
无论是气体、液体还是固体，它的分子结构都是一样的。	It has the same molecular structure whether it is a gas, liquid, or solid.
虽然它的物理状态可能会改变，但化学状态保持不变。	Although its physical state may change, its chemical state remains the same.
时间就在我们身边，影响着我们做的每一件事，但却很难理解。	Time is something that is all around us, and affects everything we do, yet is difficult to understand.
数千年来，时间一直是宗教、哲学和科学学者的研究对象。	Time has been studied by religious, philosophical, and scientific scholars for thousands of years.
我们所经历的时间是一系列从未来到现在再到过去的事件。	We experience time as a series of events passing from the future through the present to the past.
时间也是我们用来比较事件持续时间（长度）的方式。	Time is also how we compare the duration (length) of events.
你可以通过观察重复的周期性事件来记录时间的流逝。周期性事件是指有规律地一次又一次发生的事。	You can mark the passing of time yourself by observing the repetition of a cyclical event. A cyclical event is something that happens again and again regularly.
今天，我们使用计算机处理图片和视频。	Computers today are used to manipulate pictures and videos.
复杂的动画可以在计算机上构建，这种类型的动画正越来越多地应用于电视和电影。	Sophisticated animations can be constructed on computers, and this kind of animation is increasingly being used in television and films.
录制音乐时往往用复杂的计算机来处理，并把声音混合在一起。	Music is often recorded using sophisticated computers to process and mix sounds together.
在十九世纪和二十世纪很长一段时间，人们都认为新西兰的第一批居民是毛利人，他们猎取一种称为恐鸟的大型鸟类。	For a long time during the nineteenth and twentieth centuries, it was believed the first inhabitants of New Zealand were the Maori people, who hunted giant birds called moas.
然后该理论确立了这样一种观点：毛利人从波利尼西亚乘“大船”迁移，并从莫里奥里人手中夺取了新西兰，建立了一个农业社会。	The theory then established the idea that the Maori people migrated from Polynesia in a Great Fleet and took New Zealand from the Moriori, establishing an agricultural society.
但有新的证据表明，莫里奥里人属于大陆毛利人族群，他们从新西兰移居到查塔姆群岛，发展出了自己独特的崇尚和平的文化。	However, new evidence suggests that the Moriori were a group of mainland Maori who migrated from New Zealand to the Chatham Islands, developing their own distinctive, peaceful culture.
查塔姆群岛上还有另一个部落，他们是从新西兰移民过来的毛利人。	There was also another tribe on the Chatham islands these were Maori who migrated away from New Zealand.
他们自称莫里奥里人。发生过一些小冲突，最后莫里奥里人被消灭了	They called themselves the Moriori there were a few skirmishes and in the end, the Moriori were wiped out
参与了几十年的人士帮助我们认识到自己的长处和热情所在，同时坦诚地评估困难，甚至是失败。	Individuals who had been involved for several decades helped us appreciate our strengths and passions while candidly assessing difficulties and even failures.
在听取别人分享他们个人、家庭和组织的故事时，我们对过去以及一些对组织文化有或好或坏影响的人物有了宝贵的认识。	While listening to individuals share their individual, family, and organizational stories, we gained valuable insight into the past and some of the personalities who influenced for good or ill the culture of the organization.
虽然理解历史并不意味着理解文化，但至少可以帮助人们了解自己在组织历史中的位置。	While understanding one’s history does not assume understanding of culture, it does at least help people gain a sense of where they fall within the history of the organization.
在总结成功和失败时，个人和所有参与者会对组织的价值观、使命和驱动力有更深刻的认识。	While assessing the successes and becoming aware of failures, individuals and the whole of the participating persons discover more deeply the values, mission, and driving forces of the organization.
在这种情况下，回顾之前的创业行为和取得的成功可以帮助人们对当地教会的新变化和新方向保持开放的态度。	In this instance, recalling previous instances of entrepreneurial behavior and resulting successes helped people to be open to new changes and new direction for the local church.
这样的成功故事让人们对变化的恐惧感减轻了，同时为未来的变革营造出正面的倾向。	Such success stories lessened the fears of change, while creating positive inclinations toward change in the future.
收敛思维模式是通过结合不同的想法或领域来寻找解决方案的问题解决技巧。	Convergent thinking patterns are problem solving techniques that unite different ideas or fields to find a solution.
这种思维模式看重的是速度、逻辑和准确性，还有甄别事实、对现有技术的重新应用和信息收集。	The focus of this mindset is speed, logic and accuracy, also identification of facts, reapplying existing techniques, gathering information.
这种思维模式最重要的因素是：正确答案只有一个。你只需考虑两个答案，即对的或者是错的。	The most important factor of this mindset is: there is only one correct answer. You only think of two answers, namely right or wrong.
这种思维模式与某些科学或标准程序不无关联。	This type of thinking is associated with certain science or standard procedures.
这种思维类型的人具有逻辑思维，能够记得住模式、解决问题，还能进行科学测试。	People with this type of thinking have logical thinking, are able to memorize patterns, solve problems and work on scientific tests.
到目前为止，人类是最善于读懂他人心思的物种。	Humans are by far the most talented species in reading the minds of others.
这意味着我们能够成功地预测其他人的感知、意图、信仰、知识或欲望。	That means we are able to successfully predict what other humans perceive, intend, believe, know or desire.
在这些能力中，理解他人意图至关重要。我们可以凭借这一能力理解身体行为可能表达出的模棱两可的问题。	Among these abilities, understanding the intention of others is crucial. It allows us to resolve possible ambiguities of physical actions.
例如，如果你看到有人打破车窗，你很有可能会认为这个人在偷陌生人的汽车。	For example, if you were to see someone breaking a car window, you would probably assume he was trying to steal a stranger’s car.
如果他是丢了车钥匙，试图打开自己汽车的车门的话，那可能就要另当别论了。	He would need to be judged differently if he had lost his car keys and it was his own car that he was trying to break into.
磁共振成像依据的是一种叫核磁共振 (NMR) 的物理现象，它是费利克斯·布洛赫（在斯坦福大学工作）和爱德华·珀塞耳（来自哈佛大学）于 20 世纪 30 年代发现的。	MRI is based on a physics phenomenon called nuclear magnetic resonance (NMR), which was discovered in the 1930s by Felix Bloch (working at Stanford University) and Edward Purcell (from Harvard University).
在这种共振中，磁场和无线电波导致原子发出微弱的无线电信号。	In this resonance, magnetic field and radio waves cause atoms to give off tiny radio signals.
1970 年，医学博士兼研究科学家雷蒙德·达马迪安 (Raymond Damadian) 发现了使用磁共振成像作为医学诊断工具的基础原理。	In the year 1970, Raymond Damadian, a medical doctor and research scientist, discovered the basis for using magnetic resonance imaging as a tool for medical diagnosis.
四年后，一项专利获批准，这是世界上首个颁发的核磁共振领域专利。	Four years later a patent was granted, which was the world's first patent issued in the field of MRI.
1977 年，达马迪安（Damadian）博士完成了第一台 “全身” 核磁共振扫描仪的制造，他称之为 “不屈号”。	In 1977, Dr. Damadian completed the construction of the first “whole-body” MRI scanner, which he called the ”Indomitable”.
异步通讯让人们有时间思考他人的反应并作出反应。	Asynchronous communication encourages time for reflection and reaction to others.
这让学生能够按自己的节奏学习，并控制传授教学信息的节奏。	It allows students the ability to work at their own pace and control the pace of instructional information.
此外，由于可以实行弹性工作时间，时间上的限制也比较少。（布雷默，1998年）	In addition, there are fewer time restrictions with the possibility of flexible working hours. (Bremer, 1998)
学习者可以使用互联网和万维网随时获取信息。	The use of the Internet and the World Wide Web allows learners to have access to information at all times.
学生也可以在一天中的任何时间把问题提交给老师，并且可以预期得到合理时间内的快速回复，而不用一直等到下一次面谈。	Students can also submit questions to instructors at any time of day and expect reasonably quick responses, rather than waiting until the next face-to-face meeting.
后现代主义学习方法给人带来绝对的自由。并没有一种学习方法是好的学习方法。	The postmodern approach to learning offers the freedom from absolutes. There is no one good way to learn.
事实上，没有任何事情需要特意学习。在学习者体验到知识呈现的时候，学习的行为就发生了。	In fact, there is not one good thing to learn.Learning takes place in the experience between the learner and the knowledge presented.
目前我们对所有以 DIY 、展示信息以及以学习为主要内容的电视节目的体验，都说明了这一点。	Our current experience with all the do-it-yourself and information presenting, learning-based television shows illustrates this point.
我们中有很多人，都发现自己观看的电视节目在告诉我们某种过程或经验，但我们却永远不会参与或应用这些知识。	So many of us find ourselves watching a television show that informs us of a process or experience in which we will never participate or apply that knowledge.
我们永远不会对汽车进行大修，不会在后院建喷泉，不会去秘鲁考察古代遗迹，也不会改造邻居的房子。	We will never overhaul a car, build a fountain in our backyard, travel to Peru to examine ancient ruins, or remodel our neighbour's house.
多亏有了与欧洲相连的海底光缆和宽带卫星，格陵兰网络连接畅通，93% 的人口接入了互联网。	Thanks to undersea fiber optic cable links to Europe and broadband satellite, Greenland is well connected with 93% of the population having internet access.
你的酒店或房东（如果住在民宿或私人民宅）可能配有 wifi 或可联网的电脑。所有安置点都有一家网吧或有公共 wifi 的地方。	Your hotel or hosts (if staying in a guesthouse or private home) will likely have wifi or an internet connected PC, and all settlements have an internet cafe or some location with public wifi.
正如上文所提，虽然“爱斯基摩人”这个词在美国仍然可以接受，但北极地区的许多非美籍人士，尤其是对加拿大人来说，他们都认为这个词带有贬义含义。	As mentioned above, though the word "Eskimo" remains acceptable in the United States, it is considered pejorative by many non-U.S. Arctic peoples, especially in Canada.
尽管你可能会听到格陵兰本地人用这个词，但外国人应该避免使用。	While you may hear the word used by Greenlandic Natives, its use should be avoided by foreigners.
在加拿大，格陵兰岛的土著居民称自己为因纽特人，在格陵兰岛则称自己为 Kalaalleq（复数为 Kalaallit），也就是“格陵兰人”的意思。	The native inhabitants of Greenland call themselves Inuit in Canada and Kalaalleq (plural Kalaallit), a Greenlander, in Greenland.
在格陵兰岛，针对外国人的犯罪和恶意行为总体来说几乎闻所未闻。即使在城镇里，也没有 “犯罪高发区”。	Crime, and ill-will toward foreigners in general, is virtually unknown in Greenland. Even in the towns, there are no "rough areas."
严寒也许是没有准备的人将面临的唯一真正的危险。	Cold weather is perhaps the only real danger the unprepared will face.
如果你在寒冷的季节到访格陵兰岛（记住越往北走越冷），一定要带够保暖衣物。	If you visit Greenland during cold seasons (considering that the further north you go, the colder it will be), it is essential to bring warm enough clothing.
夏季漫长的白昼会导致睡眠不足和相关健康问题。	The very long days in the summer can lead to problems getting sufficient sleep and associated health issues.
在夏季，也要注意北欧的蚊子。虽然这些蚊子不会传播任何疾病，但它们可能会让人感到不适。	During the summer, also watch out for the Nordic mosquitoes. Although they do not transmit any diseases, they can be irritating.
旧金山的经济与自身是世界级旅游胜地这一点有关，但旧金山的经济却是多元化的。	While San Francisco's economy is linked to it being a world-class tourist attraction, its economy is diversified.
就业最多的部门包括专业服务业、政府、金融、贸易和旅游业。	The largest employment sectors are professional services, government, finance, trade, and tourism.
它经常出现在音乐、电影、文学和流行文化中，使得这座城市及其地标闻名于世。	Its frequent portrayal in music, films, literature and popular culture has helped make the city and its landmarks known throughout the world.
