这一“典型”的游玩过程包括飞往奥兰多国际机场，乘车前往迪士尼园区酒店，在迪士尼游玩大约一周的时间，然后回家。	The "typical" visit involves flying into Orlando International Airport, busing to an on-site Disney hotel, spending about a week without leaving Disney property, and returning home.
迪士尼的玩法有无数种，但对大多数人来说，“去迪士尼乐园”就是这个意思。	There are infinite variations possible, but this remains what most people mean when they talk of "going to Disney World".
许多在 eBay 或 Craigslist 等拍卖网站上出售的门票都是部分使用过的多日通票。	Many tickets sold online through auction websites such as eBay or Craigslist are partially used multi-day park-hopper tickets.
虽然这是一种很常见的行为，但迪士尼却禁止这样做：门票是不可转让的。	While this is a very common activity, it is prohibited by Disney: the tickets are non-transferable.
需要获得野营许可证才可以在大峡谷边缘的下方露营。	Any camping below the rim in Grand Canyon requires a backcountry permit.
为了保护大峡谷，许可证限量发放。按启程月份算起提前四个月，在该月的第一天开始发放。	Permits are limited to protect the canyon, and become available on the 1st day of the month, four months prior to the start month.
因此，如果启程日期为 5 月，野地露营许可证将在 1 月 1 日发放。	Thus, a backcountry permit for any start date in May becomes available on 1 Jan.
最受欢迎的区域比如幽灵牧场 (Phantom Ranch) 附近的光明天使 (Bright Angel) 露营地，通常在第一天开放预订时就会收到满额预订申请。	Space for the most popular areas, such as the Bright Angel Campground adjacent to Phantom Ranch, generally fill up by the requests received on first date they are opened to reservations.
对于未经预约的到访，许可证的预留数量有限，并按先到先得的原则提供许可证。	There are a limited number permits reserved for walk-in requests available on a first come, first served basis.
南部非洲非常适合开车旅行，游客既可以欣赏该地区的所有美景，又可以到达常规旅游路线之外的地方。	Entering Southern Africa by car is an amazing way to see all the region's beauty as well as to get to places off the normal tourist routes.
只要细心规划，普通汽车就能做到，但强烈建议使用四驱汽车，而且许多地方只有大轴距四驱汽车才能通过。	This can be done in a normal car with careful planning but a 4x4 is highly advised and many locations are only accessible with a high wheel base 4x4.
规划期间，请记住，虽然南部非洲处于稳定状态，但并非所有邻国亦然。	Keep in mind while planning that although Southern Africa is stable not all neighboring countries are.
签证要求和费用因国家/地区而异，并会受到你的国籍的影响。	Visa requirements and costs vary from nation to nation and are affected by the country you come from.
每个国家/地区都立有专门法律，对务必放在车内的紧急物品进行了规定。	Each country also has unique laws requiring what emergency items need to be in the car.
维多利亚瀑布镇是津巴布韦西部的一个小镇，与赞比亚的利文斯通接壤，靠近博茨瓦纳。	Victoria Falls is a town in the western portion of Zimbabwe, across the border from Livingstone, Zambia, and near Botswana.
该镇紧邻瀑布，瀑布是主要的景点，但这个热门的旅游目的地为探险者和观光者提供了可以久住的大量机会。	The town lies immediately next to the falls, and they are the major attraction, but this popular tourist destination offers both adventure seekers and sightseers plenty of opportunities for a longer stay.
在雨季（11 月至 3 月），水量会更高，瀑布也更加湍急。	In the rainy season (November to March), the water volume will be higher and the Falls will be more dramatic.
如果你过桥或沿着瀑布附近蜿蜒的小径走，肯定会被弄湿。	You are guaranteed to get wet if you cross the bridge or walk along the trails winding near the Falls.
另一方面，恰恰因为水量太大，视线会被水挡住，看不到完整的瀑布！	On the other hand, it is precisely because the volume of water is so high that your viewing of the actual Falls will be obscured—by all the water!
图坦卡蒙墓 (KV62)。 KV62 可能是山谷中最著名的墓葬。霍华德·卡特在 1922 年发现了这位年轻国王近乎完整的皇家墓葬。	Tomb of Tutankhamun (KV62). KV62 may be the most famous of the tombs in the Valley, the scene of Howard Carter's 1922 discovery of the almost intact royal burial of the young king.
但与大多数其他皇家陵墓相比，图坦卡蒙陵墓几乎不值得参观，因为它的规模要小得多，装饰也平淡无奇。	Compared to most of the other royal tombs, however, the tomb of Tutankhamun is barely worth visiting, being much smaller and with limited decoration.
如果有人想着去看这具木乃伊从棺材中移出来时受到损坏，那么这些人可要大失所望了，因为大家只能看到木乃伊的头部和肩膀。	Anyone interested in seeing evidence of the damage to the mummy done during attempts to remove it from the coffin will be disappointed as only the head and shoulders are visible.
古墓里的巨额财富已不在墓中，而是转移到了开罗的埃及博物馆。	The fabulous riches of the tomb are no longer in it, but have been removed to the Egyptian Museum in Cairo.
时间有限的游客最好选择其他去处。	Visitors with limited time would be best to spend their time elsewhere.
格罗姆寺位于暹粒市西南 12 公里处。这座山顶寺庙建于 9 世纪末耶输跋摩国王统治时期。	Phnom Krom, 12 km southwest of Siem Reap. This hilltop temple was built at the end of the 9th century, during the reign of King Yasovarman.
寺庙阴郁的氛围和洞里萨湖（Tonle Sap）的景色，让人感到爬到山顶是值得的。	The gloomy atmosphere of the temple and the view over the Tonle Sap lake make the climb to the hill worthwhile.
参观景点时，还可以顺便乘船游湖。	A visit to the site can be conveniently combined with a boat trip to the lake.
需要购买吴哥门票才能进入圣殿，所以前往洞里萨湖（Tonle Sap）时别忘了带上护照。	The Angkor Pass is needed to enter the temple so do not forget to bring your passport along when heading to Tonle Sap.
耶路撒冷是以色列的首都和最大城市，尽管大多数的其他国家/地区和联合国都不承认耶路撒冷是以色列的首都。	Jerusalem is the capital and largest city of Israel, though most other countries and the United Nations do not recognize it as Israel's capital.
坐落于犹太山丘 （Judean Hills） 上的这座古城，引人入胜的历史长达几千年之久。	The ancient city in the Judean Hills has a fascinating history spanning thousands of years.
这座城市是三大一神宗教——犹太教、基督教和伊斯兰教的圣地，是一个真正的精神、宗教和文化中心。	The city is holy to the three monotheistic religions - Judaism, Christianity and Islam, and serves as a spiritual, religious, and cultural center.
耶路撒冷（尤其是老城的许多场所）的宗教意义使这座城成为以色列主要旅游目的地之一。	Due to the religious significance of the city, and in particular the many sites of the Old City area, Jerusalem is one of the main tourist destinations in Israel.
耶路撒冷不仅有许多历史、考古和文化遗址，还有充满活力、人头涌涌的购物中心、咖啡馆和餐馆。	Jerusalem has many historic, archeological and cultural sites, along with vibrant and crowded shopping centers, cafés, and restaurants.
厄瓜多尔规定：古巴公民必须在收到邀请函后，才能通过国际机场或边境口岸进入厄瓜多尔。	Ecuador requires that Cuban citizens receive an invitation letter prior to entering Ecuador through international airports or frontier admission points.
该函必须经厄瓜多尔外交部批准，并符合某些要求。	This letter must be legalized by the Ecuadorian Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and comply with certain requirements.
这些要求是为了在两国之间实现有条不紊的移居而设计的。	These requirements are designed to provide an organized migratory flow between both countries.
持有美国绿卡的古巴公民应访问厄瓜多尔领事馆获得对此要求的豁免。	Cuban citizens who are US green card holders should visit an Ecuadorian Consulate to obtain an exemption to this requirement.
你的护照离出发日期应至少有 6 个月，而且需要一张往返/联程机票来证明你的停留时间。	Your passport must be valid for at least 6 months beyond your travel dates. A round/onward trip ticket is needed to prove the length of your stay.
旅游对人数较多的旅行团来说比较便宜。如果你独自一人或只有一个朋友同行，不妨试着认识其他人，组建 4 到 6 人的旅行团，这样可以获得更优惠的人均价格。	Tours are cheaper for larger groups, so if you're by yourself or with just one friend, try to meet other people and form a group of four to six for a better per-person rate.
不过，也有一点要担心的地方，因为游客经常被运过来运过去以把汽车坐满。	However, this shouldn't really be off your concern, because often tourists are shuffled around to fill the cars.
这实际上更像是一种骗人的方式，让人们以为他们必须支付更多的钱。	It seems actually to be more a way of tricking people into believing they have to pay more.
高耸于马丘比丘北端的这座陡峭的山峰，常常会成为许多遗址照片的背景。	Towering above the north end of Machu Picchu is this steep mountain, often the backdrop to many photos of the ruins.
从下面往上看有点吓人，而且是陡峭而艰难的上坡路，但大多数身体状况良好的人应该能在 45 分钟内完成。	It looks a bit daunting from below, and it is a steep and difficult ascent, but most reasonably fit persons should be able to make it in about 45 minutes.
小径的大部分路段都铺设了石阶；在较陡的部分还有钢缆作为支撑的扶手。	Stone steps are laid along most of the path, and in the steeper sections steel cables provide a supporting handrail.
据说会让人喘不过气来，还有在陡峭的地方要小心谨慎，特别是天气潮湿时，情况有可能很快变得很危险。	That said, expect to be out of breath, and take care in the steeper portions, especially when wet, as it can become dangerous quickly.
必须穿过靠近顶部的一个很低、很狭窄的小洞。	There's a tiny cave near the top that must be passed through, it is quite low and a rather tight squeeze.
要游览加拉帕戈斯群岛的景点和野生动植物，最好的交通方式就是乘船。查尔斯·达尔文在 1835 年就是乘船游览此地的。	Seeing the sites and wildlife of the Galapagos is best done by boat, just as Charles Darwin did it in 1835.
超过 60 艘游船在加拉帕戈斯群岛（Galapagos）水域定期往返——这些游船的体量从可承载 8 人到 100 人不等。	Over 60 cruise ships ply the Galapagos waters - ranging in size from 8 to 100 passengers.
多数人很早就提前订好位置（因为船在旺季通常会客满）。	Most people book their place well in advance (as the boats are usually full during the high season).
一定要确保你预订行程的代理是一位对各种船只拥有丰富知识的加拉帕戈斯群岛（Galapagos）专家。	Be sure the agent through whom you book is a Galapagos specialist with a good knowledge of a wide variety of ships.
这能确保你的某项兴趣和/或约束条件能与最适合他们的船只相互匹配。	This will ensure that your particular interests and/or constraints are matched with the ship most suitable to them.
在 16 世纪西班牙人到来之前，智利北部受印加统治，而土著阿拉可尼人（Araucanians）（即马普切人）则居住于智利中部和南部。	Before the Spanish arrived in the 16th century, northern Chile was under Inca rule while the indigenous Araucanians (Mapuche) inhabited central and southern Chile.
马普切人也是最后独立的美洲原住民部落之一。直到智利独立后，才完全归入西班牙语系统治者的统治下。	The Mapuche were also one of the last independent American indigenous groups, that were not fully absorbed into Spanish-speaking rule until after Chile's independence.
尽管智利在1810年宣布独立（在拿破仑战争期间，西班牙在数年中没有正常运作的中央政府），但直到1818年才取得对西班牙的决定性胜利。	Although Chile declared independence in 1810 (amid the Napoleonic wars that left Spain without a functioning central government for a couple of years), decisive victory over the Spanish was not achieved until 1818.
多米尼加共和国（西班牙语：República Dominicana）是一个加勒比国家，地处伊斯帕尼奥拉岛的东半部分，该岛分属多米尼加与海地两国	The Dominican Republic (Spanish: República Dominicana) is a Caribbean country that occupies the eastern half of the island of Hispaniola, which it shares with Haiti
除了拥有白色沙滩和山地景观，该国还是美洲地区最古老的欧洲风格城市的所在地，如今成为了圣多明各的其中一部分。	Besides white sand beaches and mountain landscapes, the country is home to the oldest European city in the Americas, now part of Santo Domingo.
泰诺人 (Taínos) 和加勒比人 (Caribes) 最先来到这个岛上定居。加勒比人是讲阿拉瓦克语 (Arawakan) 的民族，大约于公元前 10000 年来到这里。	The island was first inhabited by the Taínos and Caribes. The Caribes were an Arawakan-speaking people who had arrived around 10,000 BCE.
在欧洲探险者到来后的短短几年里，西班牙征服者就大大削减了泰诺斯的人口	Within a few short years following the arrival of European explorers, the population of Tainos had significantly been reduced by the Spanish conquerors
根据《Fray Bartolomé de las Casas》（Tratado de las Indias），1492 年至 1498 年间，西班牙侵略者杀害了约 100,000 台诺人。	Based on Fray Bartolomé de las Casas (Tratado de las Indias) between 1492 and 1498 the Spanish conquerors killed around 100,000 Taínos.
联盟花园 (Jardín de la Unión)。这里曾是一座 17 世纪修道院的中庭，其中的圣地亚哥圣殿是唯一现存的建筑。	Jardín de la Unión. This space was built as the atrium for a 17th-century convent, of which the Templo de San Diego is the sole surviving building.
现在这里成为了中心广场，昼夜都热闹繁忙。	It now functions as the central plaza, and always has a lot of things going on, day and night.
花园周围有许多餐馆，在下午和晚上，中央凉亭经常会有免费演唱会。	There are a number of restaurants surrounding the garden, and in the afternoons and evening there free concerts are often given from the central gazebo.
Callejon del Beso（亲吻小巷）。两个相隔仅 69 厘米的阳台是一个古老的爱情传说发生的地方。	Callejon del Beso (Alley of the Kiss). Two balconies separated by only 69 centimeters is home of an old love legend.
只要给一点点钱，你就能让一些孩子讲这个故事。	For a few pennies some children will tell you the story.
宝云岛是适合一日游或周末游的人气目的地，当地提供皮划艇、徒步旅行、商店、餐馆等旅游项目和服务。	Bowen Island is a popular day trip or weekend excursion offering kayaking, hiking, shops, restaurants, and more.
这个真正意义上的社区位于温哥华附近的豪湾，乘坐从温哥华市中心格兰维尔岛出发的定期水上出租车，就能轻松抵达。	This authentic community is located in Howe Sound just off Vancouver, and is easily accessed via scheduled water taxis departing Granville Island in downtown Vancouver.
对那些喜欢户外活动的人来说，必然会徒步登上 Sea to Sky。	For those who enjoy outdoor activities, a trek up the Sea to Sky corridor is essential.
因举办了 2010 年冬奥会，惠斯勒（距温哥华 1.5 小时车程）价格高昂，但却闻名遐迩。	Whistler (1.5 hour drive from Vancouver) is expensive but well-known because of the 2010 Winter Olympics.
在冬季，享受北美一些最好的滑雪场地；在夏季，尝试一些真正的山地自行车骑行。	In the winter, enjoy some of the best skiing in North America, and in the summer try some authentic mountain biking.
许可证必须提前预约。你必须持有许可证，才能在塞利纳过夜。	Permits must be reserved in advance. You must have a permit to stay overnight at Sirena.
塞丽娜（Sirena）是唯一一个除露营之外还提供宿舍住宿和热餐的护林站。La Leona、San Pedrillo 和 Los Patos 只提供露营，不提供餐饮服务。	Sirena is the only ranger station that offers dormitory lodging and hot meals in addition to camping. La Leona, San Pedrillo, and Los Patos offer only camping with no food service.
可以直接从希门尼斯港 (Puerto Jiménez) 的公园管理处获得入园许可，但不能使用信用卡	It is possible to secure park permits directly from the Ranger Station in Puerto Jiménez, but they do not accept credit cards
公园管理局只发出预计到访日期之前一个月以内的公园许可证。	The Park Service (MINAE) does not issue park permits more than one month in advance of anticipated arrival.
CafeNet El Sol 提供预约服务，收费 30 美元，而一日通票价格为 10 美元；详情请见其 Corcovado 页面。	CafeNet El Sol offers a reservation service for a fee of US$30, or $10 for one-day passes; details on their Corcovado page.
库克群岛是一个岛国，是新西兰的自由结合区，位于南太平洋中部的波利尼西亚。	The Cook Islands are an island country in free association with New Zealand, located in Polynesia, in the middle of the South Pacific Ocean.
它是一个由 15 个岛屿组成的群岛，分布在 220 万平方公里的海面上。	It is an archipelago with 15 islands spread out over 2.2 million km2 of ocean.
由于和夏威夷处于同一时区，这些岛屿有时被认为是“南方的夏威夷”。	With the same time zone as Hawaii, the islands are sometimes thought of as "Hawaii down under".
虽然规模较小，但它让一些年长的游客联想到建州之前的夏威夷，当时还没有这么多大型观光酒店和其他开发项目。	Though smaller, it reminds some elderly visitors of Hawaii before statehood without all the large tourist hotels and other development.
库克群岛没有城市，而是由 15 个不同的岛屿组成。主要的岛屿有拉罗汤加岛 (Rarotonga) 和艾图塔基岛 (Aitutaki)。	The Cook Islands do not have any cities but are composed of 15 different islands. The main ones are Rarotonga and Aitutaki.
在当今发达国家，提供豪华民宿已经上升为一种艺术形式。	In developed countries today, providing deluxe bed and breakfasts has been raised to a sort of art-form.
在高端市场上，显而易见，一众 B&B 公司主要在两个方面展开竞争：床铺和早餐。	At the top end, B&Bs obviously compete mainly on two main things: bedding and breakfast.
因而在这般上佳之所里，人们往往会发现最奢华的床上用品，也许正是一条手工制作的被子，或者是一张年代久远的床榻。	Accordingly, at the finest such establishments one is apt to find the most luxurious bedding, maybe a handmade quilt or an antique bed.
早餐可能包括当地的时令美食或主人提供的特色菜。	Breakfast may include seasonal delights of the region or the host's speciality dish.
场景可能是一栋有历史意义的古老建筑，有着古色古香的家具、修剪整齐的地面和游泳池。	The setting might be an historic old building with antique furnishings, manicured grounds and a swimming pool.
坐进自己的车，开启一段漫长的公路之旅，本身就有一种简单纯粹的吸引力。	Getting into your own car and heading off on a long road trip has an intrinsic appeal in its simplicity.
与大型车不同，你可能已经很熟悉驾驶自己的车，也知道它的局限。	Unlike larger vehicles, you are probably already familiar with driving your car and know its limitations.
在私人地产或任何规模的小镇上搭建帐篷，都很容易引起不必要的注意。	Setting up a tent on private property or in a town of any size can easily attract unwanted attention.
简而言之，开车是一种很棒的自驾游方式，但它本身不太适合“露营”。	In short, using your car is a great way to take a road trip but seldom in itself a way to "camp".
如果你有一辆较大的小型面包车、运动型休旅车、轿车或旅行车，并且座椅可以放平，那么你就可以进行汽车露营。	Car camping is possible if you have a large minivan, SUV, Sedan or Station Wagon with seats that lay down.
有些酒店的渊源可以追溯到蒸汽火车和远洋轮船的黄金时代：第二次世界大战之前，在 19 世纪或 20 世纪初。	Some hotels have a heritage from the golden age of steam railways and ocean liners; before the Second World War, in the 19th or early 20th centuries.
这些酒店是当时富人和名人的落脚处，并且通常有高档餐厅和夜生活场所。	These hotels were where the rich and the famous of the day would stay, and often had fine dining and nightlife.
传统装备、缺乏最新设施及颇具年代感的优雅韵味也是其特色。	The old fashioned fittings, the lack of the latest amenities, and a certain graceful agedness are also part of their character.
虽然它们通常是属于私人所有的，但有时也为来访的国家元首和其他政要提供住宿。	While they are usually privately owned, they sometimes accommodate visiting heads of state and other dignitaries.
一名腰缠万贯的旅客可能会考虑乘飞机环游世界，并在旅途中陆续入住许多家这样的酒店。	A traveller with piles of money might consider a round the world flight, broken up with stays in many of these hotels.
食宿交换网络是一个让旅客和其目的地城市的本地居民连接的组织。	A hospitality exchange network is the organization that connects travelers with locals in the cities they are going to visit.
加入这样的组织，通常只需要填写一张在线表格；尽管有些组织提供或要求额外的验证。	Joining such a network usually just requires filling out an online form; although some networks offer or require additional verification.
随后会提供一份纸质版和/或在线版名单，将尚有空房的房东一一列出，有时会标明其他旅客的推荐和评价信息。	A listing of available hosts is then provided either in print and/or online, sometimes with references and reviews by other travelers.
沙发冲浪成立于 2004 年 1 月。在那之前，计算机程序员凯西·芬顿 (Casey Fenton) 找到了飞往冰岛的廉价航班，但却没有住所。	Couchsurfing was founded in January 2004 after computer programmer Casey Fenton found a cheap flight to Iceland but did not have a place to stay.
他给当地大学的学生发送邮件后，提供免费住宿的邀请蜂拥而至。	He emailed students at the local university and received an overwhelming number of offers for free accommodation.
旅舍主要为年轻人提供服务，二十岁左右的年轻人便是其典型客户，但你也可以经常在那里遇到相对年长的人。	Hostels cater primarily to young people – a typical guest is in their twenties – but you can often find older travellers there too.
尽管很少有带着孩子的家庭，但一些旅舍会允许他们住单间。	Families with children are a rare sight, but some hostels do allow them in private rooms.
中国北京将成为 2022 年冬季奥运会的主办城市，这座城市也将因此成为第一个同时举办过夏季和冬季奥运会的城市。	The city of Beijing in China will be the host city of the Olympic Winter Games in 2022, which will make it the first city to have hosted both the summer and winter Olympics.
北京将举办开幕式、闭幕式和室内滑冰赛事。	Beijing will host the opening and closing ceremonies and the indoor ice events.
其他滑雪活动将在张家口太子城滑雪场举行，距离北京约 220 公里（140 英里）。	Other skiing events will be at the Taizicheng ski area in Zhangjiakou, about 220 km (140 miles) from Beijing.
大多数寺庙都有一年一度的节日，从十一月底开始，到五月中旬结束，每个寺庙的节日时间各不相同。	Most of the temples do have an Annual festival starting from November end to Mid of May, which varies according to each temple's annual calendar.
大多数寺庙节日都是为了庆祝寺庙周年纪念日、主持神的生日等寺庙大事而举办的。	Most of the temple festivals is celebrated as part of temple's anniversary or presiding deity's birthday or any other major event associated with the temple.
喀拉拉邦的寺庙节日极其有趣，通常有装饰华丽的大象游行、寺庙管弦乐队表演和其他庆典活动。	Kerala's temple festivals are very interesting to see, with regular procession of decorated elephants, temple orchestra and other festivities.
世界博览会（俗称万国博览会，简称世博）是一场展示艺术和科学的国际盛会。	A World's Fair (commonly called World Exposition, or simply Expo) is large international festival of arts and sciences.
参与国在国家展馆中举办艺术和教育展览，展示世界问题或本国的文化和历史。	Participating countries present artistic and educational displays in national pavilions to showcase world issues or their country's culture and history.
世界园艺博览会是展示花卉、植物园和与植物有关的一切。	International Horticultural Expositions are specialised events which showcase floral displays, botanical gardens and anything else to do with plants.
虽然理论上世博会可以每年举行一次（只要在不同的国家举办就行），但实际上并非如此。	Although in theory they can take place annually (so long as they are in different countries), in practice they are not.
这些项目的持续时间通常从三到六个月不等，而且是在不小于 50 公顷的场地里举行。	These events normally last anywhere between three and six months, and are held on sites no smaller than 50 hectares.
多年来，人们使用过很多不同的胶片格式。标准 35mm 胶片（36x24mm 底片）是最常见的。	There are many different film formats that have been used over the years. Standard 35 mm film (36 by 24 mm negative) is much the commonest.
如果用完了胶片，通常可以很轻易地补货，所呈现的分辨率大致与当前的数码单反相机无差。	It can usually be replenished fairly easily if you run out, and gives resolution roughly comparable to a current DSLR.
一些中画幅胶片相机使用 6x6cm 的画幅，更准确地说，是 56x56mm 的底片。	Some medium-format film cameras use a 6 by 6 cm format, more precisely a 56 by 56 mm negative.
这样一来，分辨率几乎达到了 35 mm 底片（3136 mm2 对 864）的四倍。	This gives resolution almost four times that of a 35 mm negative (3136 mm2 versus 864).
对摄影师来说，野生动物是最难拍的对象之一。好运、耐心、经验、精良的设备，缺一不可。	Wildlife is among the most challenging motifs for a photographer, and needs a combination of good luck, patience, experience and good equipment.
很多人对野生动物摄影习以为常，但就像普通摄影作品一样，一张照片胜过千言万语。	Wildlife photography is often taken for granted, but like photography in general, a picture is worth a thousand words.
拍摄野生动物通常会用到长焦镜头，不过拍鸟群或微小生物之类的对象则需要其他镜头。	Wildlife photography often requires a long telephoto lens, though things like a flock of birds or a tiny creature need other lenses.
许多珍稀动物很难找到，公园有时也有针对商业摄影的规定。	Many exotic animals are hard to find, and parks sometimes have rules about taking photographs for commercial purposes.
野生动物有的怕人，有的具有攻击性。环境可能寒冷、炎热或恶劣。	Wild animals might either be shy or aggressive. The environment might be cold, hot, or otherwise hostile.
世界上有超过 5,000 种不同的语言，其中有 20 多种语言的使用者超过了 5,000 万人。	The world has over 5,000 different languages, including more than twenty with 50 million or more speakers.
而且，书面文字往往比口头文字更容易理解。在描述地址时尤为如此，因为通常很难发清楚读音。	Written words are often easier to understand than spoken words, also. This is especially true of addresses, which are often difficult to pronounce intelligibly.
在许多国家/地区，全国的人都能说一口流利的英语，而在更多的国家/地区，人们对英语也略知一二，尤其是年轻人。	Many entire nations are completely fluent in English, and in even more you can expect a limited knowledge - especially among younger people.
如果你愿意，请想象一个曼彻斯特人、一个波士顿人、一个牙买加人和一个悉尼人围坐在多伦多的一家餐馆里吃饭。	Imagine, if you will, a Mancunian, Bostonian, Jamaican and Sydneysider sitting around a table having dinner at a restaurant in Toronto.
他们用各自独特的口音和当地的土语讲述家乡的故事，逗彼此开心。	They're regaling each other with stories from their hometowns, told in their distinct accents and local argot.
在超市购买食物通常是填饱肚子最便宜的方式。如果不具备烹饪条件，就只能选择现成的食物。	Buying food in supermarkets is usually the cheapest way to get fed. Without cooking opportunities, choices are however limited to ready-made food.
超市里成品食品的种类越来越多。有些甚至提供微波炉或其他方法用来加热食品。	Increasingly supermarkets are getting a more varied section of ready-made food. Some even provide a microwave oven or other means to heat food.
在某些国家或某些类型的商店，至少有一家餐厅（通常是非正式的）的价格相当实惠。	In some countries or types of stores there is at least one on-site restaurant, often a rather informal one with affordable prices.
把你的保险单和保险公司的详细联系方式复印几份并随身携带。	Make and carry copies of your policy and your insurer's contact details with you.
为了咨询、授权和索赔，他们需要出示保险公司的邮箱地址和国际电话号码。	They need to show the insurer's e-mail address and international phone numbers for advice/authorizations and making claims.
备好一份复印件放在行李中，并在网上另存一份副本（通过电子邮件给自己发送附件，或者存储在“云端”）。	Have another copy in your luggage and online (e-mail to yourself with attachment, or stored in the "cloud").
如果旅行时随身携带笔记本电脑或平板电脑，在内存或磁盘中存储一份副本（无需网络也可访问）。	If traveling with a laptop or tablet, store a copy in its memory or disc (accessible without the internet).
同时将保险合同/联系方式的副本交予旅伴以及归乡后愿意帮忙的亲友手中。	Also give policy/contact copies to traveling companions and relatives or friends back home willing to help.
驼鹿（也被称为麋鹿）天生不具攻击性，但如果感觉到威胁它们也会自卫。	Moose (also known as elk) aren't inherently aggressive, but will defend themselves if they perceive a threat.
有些人不把驼鹿当成潜在的危险，可能会靠得太近，将自己置于危险之中。	When people don't see moose as potentially dangerous, they may approach too closely and put themselves at risk.
适量饮用含酒精的饮料。酒精对每个人的影响都不一样，了解自己的饮酒极限非常重要。	Drink alcoholic drinks with moderation. Alcohol affects everyone differently, and knowing your limit is very important.
过量饮酒可能导致长期的健康问题，比如肝脏损伤， 甚至会导致失明和死亡。饮用非法生产的酒类时，潜在的危险性更大。	Possible long term health events from excessive drinking can include liver damage and even blindness and death. The potential danger is increased when consuming illegally produced alcohol.
非法烈酒可能含有包括甲醇在内的各种危险杂质，即使小剂量也会导致失明或死亡。	Illegal spirits can contain various dangerous impurities including methanol, which can cause blindness or death even in small doses.
眼镜在国外可能更便宜，特别是在低收入国家，那里的劳动力成本更加低廉。	Eyeglasses can be cheaper in a foreign country, especially in low-income countries where labour costs are lower.
可以考虑在本国做眼部检查（尤其是医保可以报销的情况下），然后将处方拿到其他地方去配镜。	Consider getting an eye exam at home, especially if insurance covers it, and bringing the prescription along to be filed elsewhere.
在这些地区买到的高端品牌镜架可能存在两个问题：有些可能是山寨货，而且正品进口镜架可能比在国内购买要贵。	High-end brand-name frames available in such areas may have two problems; some may be knock-offs, and the real imported ones may be more expensive than at home.
咖啡是全球交易量最大的商品之一，你在家乡很可能可以买到种类繁多的咖啡。	Coffee is one of the world's most traded commodities, and you can probably find many types in your home region.
尽管如此，世界上还是有许多独特的咖啡饮用方式，这些方式都值得去体验。	Nevertheless, there are many distinctive ways of drinking coffee around the world that are worth experiencing.
溪降时要进入峡谷的底部，峡谷可以是干涸的，也可以有很深的水。	Canyoning (or: canyoneering) is about going in a bottom of a canyon, which is either dry or full of water.
溪降结合了游泳、爬山和跳跃的元素——但只需要相对较少的训练和体能基础就可以入门（和攀岩、水肺潜水、高山滑雪等相比）。	Canyoning combines elements from swimming, climbing and jumping--but requires relatively little training or physical shape to get started (compared to rock climbing, scuba diving or alpine skiing, for example).
远足是指在自然环境中（通常是在远足步道上）行走的户外活动。	Hiking is an outdoor activity which consists of walking in natural environments, often on hiking trails.
单日徒步是指一天内走完的行程，行程距离可低至少于一英里。	Day hiking involves distances of less than a mile up to longer distances that can be covered in a single day.
沿着一条平缓的小径远足一天几乎不需要什么准备，并且任何人只要身体不算差，都可以享受远足的乐趣。	For a day hike along an easy trail little preparations are needed, and any moderately fit person can enjoy them.
有小孩的家庭可能需要做更多的准备，但即使带着婴儿和学龄前儿童，在户外待一天也不难。	Families with small children may need more preparations, but a day outdoors is easily possible even with babies and pre-school children.
全球有近 200 个跑步旅游组织，大多独立运营。	Internationally, there are nearly 200 running tour organizations. Most of them operate independently.
全球跑步之旅 (Global Running Tours) 的接替者 Go Running Tours 把四大洲数十个观光跑运营商连接起来。	The Global Running Tours successor, Go Running Tours networks dozens of sightrunning providers on four continents.
这个组织起源于巴塞罗那的“巴塞罗那跑步之旅”（Running Tours Barcelona ）组织和哥本哈根的“哥本哈根跑步”（Running Copenhagen）组织，很快布拉格的“布拉格跑步之旅”（ Running Tours Prague）及其他地区的组织也加入其中。	With roots in Barcelona's Running Tours Barcelona and Copenhagen's Running Copenhagen, it was quickly joined by Running Tours Prague based in Prague and others.
出发前和旅途中，你必须考虑到很多方面。	There are many things you have to take into consideration before and when you travel somewhere.
当你旅行时，请不要期待一切就像“在家里”一样。 礼节、法律、饮食、交通、住宿、标准和语言等等都会与你居住的地方有所不同。	When you travel, expect things not to be like they are "back home". Manners, laws, food, traffic, lodging, standards, language and so on will to some extent differ from where you live.
这是你需要永远记在心上的一点，这样才能避免失望或者甚至对当地的做法表示厌恶。	This is something you always need to keep in mind, to avoid disappointment or perhaps even distaste over local ways to do things.
旅行社自 19 世纪一直存在至今。如果在一段旅程中，旅行者不熟悉目的地的自然、文化和语言，或者计划去低收入国家旅行，那么旅行社一般会是很好的选择。	Travel agencies have been around since the 19th century. A travel agent is usually a good option for a journey which extends beyond a traveller's previous experience of nature, culture, language or low-income countries.
虽然大多数旅行社都愿意接受大部分的常规预约，但也有很多旅行社专门从事特定类型、特定预算范围或特定目的地的旅行业务。	Although most agencies are willing to take on most regular bookings, many agents specialise in particular types of travel, budget ranges or destinations.
最好找一个常常预订与你的旅程类似的代理。	It can be better to use an agent who frequently books similar trips to yours.
看看旅行社推广什么旅游产品，可以在网站上或商店橱窗里查看。	Take a look at what trips the agent is promoting, whether on a website or in a shop window.
无论是出于必要、还是为了换换生活方式、挑战自我，如果你想花最少的钱看世界，有些办法可以帮你做到。	If you want to see the world on the cheap, for necessity, lifestyle or challenge, there are some ways to do that.
基本上，它们可分为两类：要么边旅行边工作，要么尽量减少开支。这篇文章着重于后者。	Basically, they fall into two categories: Either work while you travel or try and limit your expenses. This article is focused on the latter.
对于那些愿意牺牲舒适度和时间，喜欢充满惊喜的旅行，并把开销降至接近于零的游客，请参阅《最低预算旅行攻略》。	For those willing to sacrifice comfort, time and predictability to push expenses down close to zero, see minimum budget travel.
该设想假定旅行者不会为了自己的利益而进行偷窃、非法侵入、参与非法市场、乞讨或为了私利剥削他人。	The advice assumes that travellers do not steal, trespass, participate in the illegal market, beg, or otherwise exploit other people for their own gain.
入境检查站通常是走下飞机、轮船或其他交通工具后经过的第一站。	An immigration checkpoint is usually the first stop when disembarking from a plane, a ship, or another vehicle.
一些跨境列车的查验在车上进行；登上跨境列车时，应该携带有效的身份证件。	In some cross-border trains inspections are done on the running train and you should have valid ID with you when boarding one of those trains.
在夜间卧铺列车上，为了不影响乘客睡眠，列车长可能会提前收取护照。	On night sleeper trains, passports may be collected by the conductor so that you do not have your sleep interrupted.
注册是签证流程的附加要求。在一些国家，你必须向当地政府登记你的存在和住址。	Registration is an additional requirement for the visa process. In some countries, you must register your presence and address where you are staying with the local authorities.
这可能需要去当地警察局填写表格或去一趟移民办公室。	This might require filling out a form with the local police or a visit to the immigration offices.
在很多有这样法律的国家，当地的旅馆可以办理登记注册手续（一定要问清楚）。	In many countries with such a law, local hotels will handle the registration (make sure to ask).
在其他情况下，只有住在旅游住宿设施以外的人需要登记。不过这样一来，法律模糊了很多，所以要事先了解。	In other cases, only those staying outside of tourist accommodations need to register.  However, this makes the law much more obscure, so find out beforehand.
建筑学是一门研究建筑设计和建造的学科。一个地方的建筑往往本身就是旅游景点。	Architecture is concerned with the design and construction of buildings. The architecture of a place is often a tourist attraction in its own right.
许多建筑物的外观都很漂亮，无论是从高楼上看去，还是从一个位置巧妙的窗口望出去，都会看到一幅美不胜收的景象。	Many buildings are quite beautiful to look at and the view from a tall building or from a cleverly-positioned window can be a beauty to behold.
建筑与城市规划、土木工程、装饰艺术、室内设计和景观设计等领域有相当多的重叠之处。	Architecture overlaps considerably with other fields including urban planning, civil engineering, decorative arts, interior design and landscape design.
鉴于许多普韦布洛人居住得非常偏远，你得前往阿尔伯克基或圣达菲才能享受到丰富的夜生活。	Given how remote many of the pueblos are, you won't be able to find a significant amount of nightlife without traveling to Albuquerque or Santa Fe.
然而，上面列出的几乎所有赌场都供应饮料，其中一些赌场还提供知名的娱乐活动（主要是紧邻阿尔伯克基和圣达菲的大型赌场）。	However, nearly all of the casinos listed above serve drinks, and several of them bring in name-brand entertainment (primarily the large ones immediately surrounding Albuquerque and Santa Fe).
注意：对来自其他州的游客而言，这里的小镇酒吧并不总是闲逛的好地方。	Beware: small-town bars here are not always good places for the out-of-state visitor to hang out.
首先，新墨西哥州北部有严重的酒驾问题，并且小镇酒吧附近的司机酒驾的比例很高。	For one thing, northern New Mexico has significant problems with drunk driving, and the concentration of intoxicated drivers is high close to small-town bars.
擅自绘制的壁画或乱写乱涂被称为涂鸦。	Unwanted murals or scribble is known as graffiti.
尽管这绝不是现代才出现的现象，但大多数人很可能会将其与年轻人使用喷漆破坏公共和私有财产联系起来。	While it's far from a modern phenomenon, most people probably associate it with youth vandalizing public and private property using spray paint.
然而，如今已经有了成熟的涂鸦艺术家、涂鸦活动和“合法”涂鸦墙。在这种背景下创作的涂鸦绘画往往更类似于艺术品，而非难以辨认的标签。	However, nowadays there are established graffiti artists, graffiti events and "legal" walls. Graffiti paintings in this context often resemble artworks rather than illegible tags.
投掷回旋镖是很多游客都想学会的一项热门技能。	Boomerang throwing is a popular skill that many tourists want to acquire.
如果你想学掷回力镖，让它飞出去之后能飞回手中，请务必使用可以飞回的合适的回力镖。	If you want to learn throwing a boomerang that comes back to your hand, make sure you have a suitable boomerang for returning.
实际上，澳大利亚市面上的大多数回旋镖都飞不回来。初学者最好不要尝试在大风中投掷回旋镖	Most boomerangs available in Australia are in fact non-returning. It is best for beginners to not try throwing in windy
Hangi 指的是烧窑美食。	A Hangi Meal is cooked in a hot pit in the ground.
坑洞通过用火烧过的石头加热，在某些地方则是利用地热使地面自然变热。	The pit is either heated with hot stones from a fire, or in some places geothermal heat makes areas of ground naturally hot.
石头火锅经常用于烹饪传统的烤肉大餐。	The hangi is often used to cook a traditional roast style dinner.
罗托鲁瓦有几个地方提供地热窑烤 (hangi)，而在克赖斯特彻奇、惠灵顿和其他地方也可以品尝到其他做法的毛利窑烤。	Several places in Rotorua offer geothermal hangi, while other hangi can be sampled in Christchurch, Wellington and elsewhere.
开普敦城内和绕城的通勤火车上有 MetroRail 车厢，MetroRail 有两个等级：MetroPlus（也叫头等舱）和Metro（也叫三等舱）。	MetroRail has two classes on commuter trains in and around Cape Town: MetroPlus (also called First Class) and Metro (called Third Class).
MetroPlus 更舒适，也没那么拥挤，但稍微贵了一点，即便如此还是比欧洲的普通地铁票便宜。	MetroPlus is more comfortable and less crowded but slightly more expensive, though still cheaper than normal metro tickets in Europe.
每列火车都有 MetroPlus 和 Metro 车厢；前者总是在火车靠近开普敦的那一端。	Every train has both MetroPlus and Metro coaches; the MetroPlus coaches are always on the end of the train nearest Cape Town.
为他人携带物品——千万不要让行李离开你的视线，尤其是在出入境时。	Carrying for others - Never let your bags out of your sight, especially when you are crossing international borders.
你可能会发现自己被人利用，在不知情的情况下成了一个运毒者，这会让你陷入很大的麻烦。	You could find yourself being used as a drug carrier without your knowledge, which will land you in a great deal of trouble.
这包括排队等候，因为随时都可能在没有事先通知的情况下使用缉毒犬。	This includes waiting in line, as drug-sniffing dogs could be used at any time without notice.
有些国家/地区甚至对初犯也会判以极其严厉的处罚；处罚可能包括 10 年以上的监禁或死刑。	Some countries have exceedingly draconian punishments even for first time offenses; these can include prison sentences of over 10 years or death.
无人看管的袋子不仅是窃贼的目标，还会被当成炸弹威胁，引起当局的警惕和关注。	Unattended bags are a target for theft and can also attract attention from authorities wary of bomb threats.
在家时，由于会经常接触当地病菌，你极易对其产生免疫力。	At home, due to this constant exposure to the local germs, odds are very high that you're already immune to them.
但在从来没有过细菌群的世界其他地方，你遇到问题的可能性要大得多。	But in other parts of the world, where the bacteriological fauna are new to you, you're far more likely to run into problems.
而且，在温暖的气候下细菌既可以快速繁殖，又可以在体外存活更久。	Also, in warmer climates bacteria both grow more quickly and survive longer outside the body.
于是“德里腹泻”、”法老的诅咒”和“蒙特祖玛的复仇”之类的灾祸就出现了。	Thus the scourges of Delhi Belly, the Pharaoh's Curse, Montezuma's Revenge, and their many friends.
正如寒冷气候易发呼吸道问题，炎热气候也极易引发肠道问题。在绝大多数情况下，肠道问题会令人显著不适，但并非十分危险。	As with respiratory problems in colder climates, intestinal problems in hot climates are fairly common and in most cases are distinctly annoying but not really dangerous.
如果你第一次去发展中国家旅行，或者去一个陌生的地方旅行，千万不要低估可能出现的文化冲击。	If traveling in a developing country for the first time – or in a new part of the world – don't underestimate the potential culture shock.
许多情绪稳定、能力较强的旅客都曾被在发展中国家旅行的新问题所吓倒，在那里，需要迅速适应接踵而至的许多细微文化差异。	Many a stable, capable traveler has been overcome by the newness of developing world travel, where many little cultural adjustments can add up quickly.
尤其是在刚开始的日子里，您可以考虑在西式和高质量的酒店、食物和服务上多花些钱，来帮助您适应环境。	Especially in your initial days, consider splurging on Western-style and -quality hotels, food, and services to help acclimatize.
在不了解当地动物群的地区，切勿睡在地上的床垫或垫子上。	Do not sleep on a mattress or pad on the ground in areas where you do not know the local fauna.
如果要去野营，请带上露营床或吊床，以免蛇和蝎子之类的危害。	If you are going to camp out, bring a camp cot or hammock to keep you away from snakes, scorpions and such.
清晨在家享受香浓咖啡，夜晚则泡上令人放松的甘菊茶。	Fill your home with a rich coffee in the morning and some relaxing chamomile tea at night.
宅在家里度假，手头上时间多了，可以稍微多花点时间泡一杯特别的饮品，犒劳犒劳自己。	When you're on a staycation, you have the time to treat yourself and take a few extra minutes to brew up something special.
如果你想更新奇一点，可以利用这个机会榨些果汁或制作混合奶昔：	If you're feeling more adventurous, take the opportunity to juice or blend up some smoothies:
也许你会发现一种在回归到规律的日常生活时，可以在早餐时制作的简单饮料。	maybe you'll discover a simple beverage that you can make for breakfast when you're back to your daily routine.
如果你生活的城市有多种饮酒文化，那就去那些你不常去的街区的酒吧或酒馆。	If you live in a city with a varied drinking culture, go to bars or pubs in neighborhoods you don't frequent.
对于那些不熟悉医学术语的人来说，”传染性”和“触染性”这两个词的含义截然不同。	For those unfamiliar with medical jargon, the words infectious and contagious have distinct meanings.
传染病是由包括病毒、细菌、真菌和其他寄生物在内的病原体引起的疾病。	An infectious disease is one that is caused by a pathogen, such as a virus, bacterium, fungus or other parasites.
传染病是指在感染者附近极易传播的一类疾病。	A contagious disease is a disease which is easily transmitted by being in the vicinity of an infected person.
多国政府要求入境游客或离境居民接种一系列疾病疫苗。	Many governments require visitors entering, or residents leaving, their countries to be vaccinated for a range of diseases.
这些要求通常取决于旅行者已经访问或打算访问的国家。	These requirements may often depend on what countries a traveller has visited or intends to visit.
北卡罗来纳州夏洛特市的优势之一在于它为家庭提供了许多高质量的选择。	One of strong points of Charlotte, North Carolina, is that it has an abundance of high-quality options for families.
来自其他地区的住户常常评赞，家庭友好是他们移居那里的主要原因，而游客们也会发现带着孩子一起游览这座城市非常惬意。	Residents from other areas often cite family-friendliness as a primary reason for moving there, and visitors often find the city easy to enjoy with children around.
过去 20 年来，夏洛特上城区方便儿童的设施实现了指数级增长。	In the past 20 years, the amount of child-friendly options in Uptown Charlotte has grown exponentially.
在夏洛特 (Charlotte) 生活的家庭除了特殊情况外，一般不使用出租车。	Taxis are not generally used by families in Charlotte, though they can be of some use in certain circumstances.
乘客超过 2 人则需要额外付费，所以这个选项可能比较昂贵，没有必要。	There is a surcharge for having more than 2 passengers, so this option might be more expensive than necessary.
南极洲环绕着南极，是地球上最冷的地方。	Antarctica is the coldest place on Earth, and surrounds the South Pole.
旅行费用高昂，对身体素质要求也很高，并且只能在十一月至次年二月的夏季前往，游览地点主要限于半岛、群岛和罗斯海。	Tourist visits are costly, demand physical fitness, can only take place in summer Nov-Feb, and are largely limited to the Peninsula, Islands and Ross Sea.
在夏天，这里的四十余个基地会迎来几千名工作人员，其中的大多数人驻扎在此地区；一小部分人留下越冬。	A couple of thousand staff live here in summer in some four dozen bases mostly in those areas; a small number stay over winter.
南极洲内陆是一片荒凉的高原，为 2-3 千米厚的冰所覆盖。	Inland Antarctica is a desolate plateau covered by 2-3 km of ice.
偶尔会有专门的航空旅行团前往内陆旅行，参加登山活动，或前往南北极的大型基地。	Occasional specialist air tours go inland, for mountaineering or to reach the Pole, which has a large base.
南极穿越公路 (South Pole Traverse)（或高速公路）始于罗斯海的麦克默多站 (McMurdo Station)，直通南极点，全长 1600 公里。	The South Pole Traverse (or Highway) is a 1600 km trail from McMurdo Station on the Ross Sea to the Pole.
雪被压实，缝隙也被填满，并用旗帜做了标记。只有专门的拖拉机以及拖着装有燃料和补给的雪橇才能通行。	It's compacted snow with crevasses filled in and marked by flags. It can only be traveled by specialized tractors, hauling sleds with fuel and supplies.
车子并不是很灵活，所以必须绕着横贯南极山脉，拐一个长长的的大弯才能来到高原。	These aren't very nimble so the trail has to take a long swerve around the Transantarctic Mountains to come onto the plateau.
冬天最常见的事故原因是道路和路面（人行道）湿滑，特别是台阶。	The most common cause for accidents in winter is slippery roads, pavements (sidewalks) and especially steps.
至少你需要鞋底适当的鞋子。穿夏季鞋在冰雪上行走通常很滑，甚至一些冬季靴也有所不足。	At a minimum, you need footwear with suitable soles. Summer shoes are usually very slippery on ice and snow, even some winter boots are deficient.
鞋纹应该足够深，在5 毫米（1/5英寸）或以上；材料应在低温下足够柔软。	The pattern should be deep enough, 5 mm (1/5 inch) or more, and the material soft enough in cold temperatures.
有的靴子有鞋钉；也有为湿滑路面设计的、带有鞋钉的扩展装备，适用于大多数鞋子和靴子，能装在鞋跟上，或同时装在鞋跟和鞋底上。	Some boots have studs and there is studded add-on equipment for slippery conditions, suitable for most shoes and boots, for the heels or heels and sole.
鞋跟应该低而宽。道路上经常会撒上细沙、砂石或盐粒（氯化钙），以增加摩擦力。	Heels should be low and wide. Sand, gravel or salt (calcium chloride) is often scattered on roads or paths to improve traction.
雪崩并不是异常现象；陡坡上所能容纳的雪量有限，多余的雪就会以雪崩的形式坠落。	Avalanches are not an abnormality; steep slopes can hold only so much slow, and the excess volumes will come down as avalanches.
问题是雪有很强的粘性。因此需要一些触发因素才能降雪，而有一点雪落下来也可能触发其他的雪下降。	The problem is that snow is sticky, so it needs some triggering to come down, and some snow coming down can be the triggering event for the rest.
有时起初的触发原因是太阳让雪变暖，有时是因为降雪多了些，有时是因为其他自然事件，但更常见的原因往往是人为因素。	Sometimes the original trigging event is the sun warming the snow, sometimes some more snowfall, sometimes other natural events, often a human.
龙卷风是一股气压极低的旋转气流柱，它能将周围的空气向内、向上吸入。	A tornado is a spinning column of very low-pressure air, which sucks the surrounding air inward and upward.
龙卷风会产生强风（常常每小时 100-200 英里），能把重物抛到空中，并裹挟着它们向前移动。	They generate high winds (often 100-200 miles/hour) and can lift heavy objects into the air, carrying them as the tornado moves.
刚开始时，漏斗状云从雷暴云中向下伸展，当它们接触地面时就变成了“龙卷风”。	They begin as funnels descending from storm clouds, and become "tornadoes" when they touch the ground.
个人 VPN（虚拟专用网络）程序是规避政治审查和商业 IP 地理过滤的绝佳工具。	Personal VPN (virtual private network) providers are an excellent way of circumventing both political censorship and commercial IP-geofiltering.
它们优于网页代理的原因如下：它们重新路由所有互联网流量，而不仅仅是超文本传送协议 (http) 内容。	They are superior to web proxies for several reasons: They re-route all Internet traffic, not only http.
它们通常会提供更高的带宽和更优质的服务。它们经过加密，更难被监视。	They normally offer higher bandwidth and better quality of service. They are encrypted and thus harder to spy on.
媒体公司照例撒谎以掩盖其目的，声称这是为了“防止盗版”。	The media companies routinely lie about the purpose of this, claiming that it is to "prevent piracy".
事实上，区域码对非法复制毫无影响；一份逐位拷贝的磁盘副本在任何可以播放原盘的设备上都可以顺利播放。	In fact, region codes have absolutely no effect on illegal copying; a bit-for-bit copy of a disk will play just fine on any device where the original will.
实际上的目的是为了让这些公司更好地控制他们的市场；一切都是为了圈钱。	The actual purpose is to give those companies more control over their markets; it's all about money spinning.
因为呼叫是通过互联网路由的，因此你不必使用位于你居住地或旅行地点的通话公司。	Because calls are routed over the Internet, you do not need to use a phone company located where you live or where you travel.
是否在居住的社区获得本地号码，这点没有要求；你可以在阿拉斯加奇金的野外获得卫星互联网连接，然后选一个号码，显示你位于阳光明媚的亚利桑那州。	There is also no requirement that you obtain a local number from the community in which you live; you can obtain a satellite Internet connection in the wilds of Chicken, Alaska and select a number which claims you're in sunny Arizona.
很多时候，你必须单独购买一个可以在全球使用的号码，这样才能接听来自公共交换电话网 (PSTN) 电话的呼叫。该号码的来源地对主叫方有很大影响。	Often, you have to buy a global number separately that allows PSTN phones to call you. Where the number is from makes a difference for people calling you.
实时文本翻译应用：能够自动将整段文本从一种语言转换成另一种语言的应用程序。	Real-time text translator apps – applications that are capable of automatically translating whole segments of text from one language into another.
某些此类应用程序甚至让用户把智能手机对着现实世界中的标志或其他物体，就能翻译上面的外语文字。	Some of the applications in this category can even translate texts in foreign languages on signs or other objects in the real world when the user points the smartphone towards those objects.
翻译引擎有了显著的改进，现在经常提供或多或少正确的翻译（而更多情况是很少有胡言乱语），但需要注意的是，他们仍然可能会完全翻错。	The translation engines have improved dramatically, and now often give more or less correct translations (and more seldom gibberish), but some care is due, as they still may have gotten it all wrong.
一个最杰出的此类应用是谷歌翻译。在下载所需语言数据后，它可以进行离线翻译。	One of the most prominent apps in this category is Google Translate, which allows offline translation after downloading the desired language data.
出国旅行时，使用智能手机 GPS 导航应用可能是最简单方便的导航方式。	Using GPS navigation apps on your smartphone can be the easiest and most convenient way to navigate when out of your home country.
比起够买带 GPS 的地图或独立的 GPS 设备，或者是从汽车租赁公司租一个，这种方式更省钱。	It can save money over buying new maps for a GPS, or a standalone GPS device or renting one from a car rental company.
如果你的手机没有数据连接，或者不在服务范围，手机的性能可能会受限，或者无法使用手机。	If you don't have a data connection for your phone, or when it is out of range, their performance can be limited or unavailable.
每个街头小店都摆满了一排令人眼花缭乱的预付费电话卡，这些电话卡既可以用于公用付费电话机，也可以用于普通电话机。	Every corner store is filled with a confusing array of pre-paid phone cards that can be used from pay phones or ordinary telephones.
尽管大多数电话卡适合给任何地方打电话，但有些卡在拨打一些特定国家的电话时有特别优惠。	While most cards are good for calling anywhere, some specialise in providing favourable call rates to specific groups of countries.
通常拨打一个电话号码即可获取这些服务，而大多数的电话都可免费拨打该串号码。	Access to these services is often through a toll-free telephone number that can be called from most phones without charge.
有关常规摄影的规则也适用于录像，甚至可能更适用。	Rules regarding regular photography also apply to video recording, possibly even more so.
如果连拍照都不允许的话，就更不用想拍摄视频了。	If just taking a photo of something isn't allowed, then you shouldn't even think of recording a video of it.
如果使用无人机，请提前仔细确认可以拍摄的内容，以及需要哪些许可或额外的牌照。	If using a drone, check well in advance as to what you are allowed to film and what permits or additional licensing are required.
在机场附近或人群拥挤的地方操控无人机升空，是个馊主意，即使这在你所在地区并不违法。	Flying a drone near an airport or over a crowd is almost always a bad idea, even if it's not illegal in your area.
现在已经很少有人不先搜索和比较价格，就直接通过航空公司订票了。	Nowadays air travel is only rarely booked directly through the airline without first searching and comparing prices.
有时，同一航班在不同信息汇集网站上的价格可能相差很大，在预订前先比较搜索结果，同时看看航空公司自己的网站，是有好处的。	Sometimes the same flight can have vastly differing prices at various agregators and it pays to compare search results and to also look at the website of the airline itself before booking.
尽管短期访问某些国家时，旅游或商务出行并不需要签证，但留学生去那里的话，所待的时间通常需比休闲的游客要长。	While you may not need a visa for short visits to certain countries as a tourist or for business, going there as an international student generally requires a longer stay than going there just as a casual tourist.
通常来说，较长时间停留在外国需要提前获取签证。	In general, staying in any foreign country for an extended period of time will require you to obtain a visa in advance.
与普通旅游签证或商务签证相比，学生签证通常有不同的要求和申请程序。	Student visas generally have different requirements and application procedures from normal tourist or business visas.
在大多数国家，你需要一份你希望就读的学校的录取通知书，以及证明你有至少第一年课程所需资金的文件。	For most countries, you will need an offer letter from the institution you wish to study at, and also evidence of funds to support yourself for at least the first year of your course.
咨询学校及你希望留学的国家的移民局，以了解详细要求。	Check with the institution, as well as the immigration department for the country you wish to study in for detailed requirements.
除非你是外交官，否则在海外工作一般需要向所在国家/地区缴纳所得税。	Unless you are a diplomat, working overseas generally means that you will have to file income tax in the country you are based in.
国家不同，所得税的结构是不同的，税率和税率等级也有很大的差异。	Income tax is structured differently in different countries, and the tax rates and brackets vary widely from one country to another.
一些联邦国家，比如美国和加拿大，会征收联邦和地方所得税，因此税率和等级可能因地区而异。	In some federal countries, such as the United States and Canada, income tax is levied both at the federal level and at the local level, so the rates and brackets can vary from region to region.
在回到本国时通常不需要进行入境检查或者只是走走形式，但过海关可能会很麻烦。	While immigration check is usually absent or a formality when you arrive in your homeland, customs control can be a hassle.
确保知晓可以携带什么，不能携带什么，并申报任何超出法律允许的物件。	Make sure you know what you can and cannot bring in and declare anything over the legal limits.
开始旅行写作最简单的方法就是在一个资深旅行博客网站上磨练你的技能。	The easiest way to get started in the business of travel writing is to hone your skills on an established travel blog website.
熟悉网上排版和编辑后，你便可创建自己的网站。	After you become comfortable with formatting and editing on the web, then later, you might create your own website.
在旅行中进行志愿服务是一种与众不同的好方法，但这不仅仅在于付出。	Volunteering while travelling is a great way to make a difference but it's not just about giving.
在国外生活和做志愿者，是了解不同文化、结识新朋友、了解自我、锻炼正确判断的能力、甚至是获得新技能的好方法。	Living and volunteering in a foreign country is a great way to get to know a different culture, meet new people, learn about yourself, get a sense of perspective and even gain new skills.
这也是一个节省预算的好方法，可以在某处待更长时间，因为很多志愿者工作提供食宿，有些工作还有少量工资。	It can also be a good way to stretch a budget to allow a longer stay somewhere since many volunteer jobs provide room and board and a few pay a small salary.
维京人利用俄罗斯水路到达黑海和里海。其中一些路线至今仍可通行。确认一下是否需要特殊许可证，这些许可证可能很难申请。	Vikings used the Russian waterways to get to the Black Sea and Caspian Sea. Parts of these routes can still be used. Check possible need for special permits, which may be difficult to get.
白令海峡经由奥内加湖（Lake Onega）、拉多加湖（Lake Ladoga）和圣彼得堡（Saint Petersburg）连接北冰洋和波罗的海，连接处多数是河流和湖泊。	The White Sea–Baltic Canal connects the Arctic Ocean to the Baltic Sea, via Lake Onega, Lake Ladoga and Saint Petersburg, mostly by rivers and lakes.
奥内加湖 (Lake Onega) 也与伏尔加河 (Volga) 连接，因此可能可以从里海 (Caspian Sea) 经俄罗斯到达这里。	Lake Onega is also connected to Volga, so coming from the Caspian Sea through Russia is still possible.
请放心，在到达码头后，一切都会顺其自然。你会遇到其他要搭便船的人，他们会与你分享信息。	Be assured that once you hit the marinas everything will be pretty obvious. You will meet other boat hitchhikers and they will share their information with you.
基本上，你可以张贴告示，告知他人你可以提供帮助、在码头上来回走动、接触正在清理游艇的人或酒吧里的水手等等。	Basically you'll be putting up notices offering your help, pacing the docks, approaching people cleaning their yachts, trying to make contact with sailors in the bar, etc.
试着和尽可能多的人聊天。过一段时间，每个人都会认识你，他们会提示你哪条船在找人。	Try to talk to as many people as possible. After a while everyone will know you and will give you hints as to which boat is looking for someone.
你务必谨慎选择联盟中的”飞行常客“航空公司。	You should choose your Frequent Flyer airline in an alliance carefully.
虽然你可能会认为，乘坐哪家航空公司航班的次数最多就加入哪家航空公司的会员是很自然的事，但你应该知道，航空公司提供的权益往往不同，同一联盟下的其他航空公司可能会回馈更多常旅客积分。	Although you may think it is intuitive to join the airline you fly most, you should be aware that privileges offered are often different and frequent flyer points may be more generous under a different airline in the same alliance.
诸如阿联酋航空公司、阿提哈德航空公司、卡塔尔航空公司和土耳其航空公司之类的航司已经大大扩展了对非洲的服务业务，提供了飞往非洲许多主要城市的航线，价格也比其他欧洲航空公司更有竞争力。	Airlines such as Emirates, Etihad Airways, Qatar Airways & Turkish Airlines have greatly expanded their services to Africa, and offer connections to many major African cities at competitive rates than other European airlines.
从 2014 年开始，土耳其航空公司可到达 30 个非洲国家的 39 个目的地。	Turkish Airlines flies to 39 destinations in 30 African countries as of 2014.
如果你的旅行时间有富余，请查看前往非洲的总票价跟环球旅行票价的比较情况。	If you have additional travel time, check to see how your total fare quote to Africa compares with a round-the-world fare.
对于非洲以外的所有地区，别忘了加上额外的签证费、离境税、地面交通等费用。	Don't forget to add in the extra costs of additional visas, departure taxes, ground transportation, etc. for all those places outside of Africa.

南半球没有一家航空联盟的航线能横跨全部三个大洋（天合联盟甚至没有跨洋航线）。	No airline alliance covers all three ocean crossings in the Southern Hemisphere (and SkyTeam covers none of the crossings).

运河区（荷兰语：Grachtengordel）是阿姆斯特丹宾嫩斯塔 (Binnenstad) 周围著名的 17 世纪老城区。	The Canal District (Dutch: Grachtengordel) is the famous 17th-century district surrounding the Binnenstad of Amsterdam.
由于独特的文化和历史价值，整个地区被联合国教科文组织列为世界遗产，该区的房产价值位居该国的最高之列。	The whole district is designated as a UNESCO World Heritage Site for its unique cultural and historical value, and its property values are among the highest of the country.
五渔村（Cinque Terre），原意为五块土地，由位于意大利利古里亚（Liguria）地区的五座沿海小村庄 Riomaggiore、Manarola、Corniglia、Vernazza 和 Monterosso 组成。	Cinque Terre, which means Five Lands, comprises the five small coastal villages of Riomaggiore, Manarola, Corniglia, Vernazza and Monterosso located in the Italian region of Liguria.
它们被列入了联合国教科文组织世界遗产名录。	They are listed on the UNESCO World Heritage List.
几个世纪以来，人们在崎岖陡峭的地形上精心建造梯田，这些山坡一直延伸到俯瞰大海的悬崖峭壁。	Over the centuries, people have carefully built terraces on the rugged, steep landscape right up to the cliffs that overlook the sea.
它的魅力部分在于没有明显的企业发展。村庄靠道路、火车和船只连接起来，开车无法从外面到达这些村庄。	Part of its charm is the lack of visible corporate development. Paths, trains and boats connect the villages, and cars cannot reach them from the outside.
比利时和瑞士使用的法语语种与法国使用的法语尽管非常相似，可以互通，但还是稍有不同。	The varieties of French which are spoken in Belgium and Switzerland differ slightly from the French spoken in France, though they are similar enough to be mutually intelligible.
具体说来，比利时和瑞士讲的法语在数字系统上有一些细微的特殊性，与法国讲的法语不同，一些单词的发音也略有不同。	In particular, the numbering system in French-speaking Belgium and Switzerland has some slight peculiarities that are different from the French spoken in France, and the pronunciation of some words is slightly different.
不过，所有说法语的比利时人和瑞士人都会在学校里学习标准法语，所以即使您使用标准的法国度量系统，他们也能听得懂。	Nevertheless, all French-speaking Belgians and Swiss would have learned standard French in school, so they would be able to understand you even if you used the standard French numbering system.
在世界上许多地方，挥手是一种友好的表示，意思是“你好”。	In many parts of the world, waving is a friendly gesture, indicating "hello."
但是，在马来西亚，至少在农村地区的马来人中，这个手势类似于在某些西方国家用食指朝自己身体摆动，表示“过来”，并且这个手势仅用来表示这个意思。	However, in Malaysia, at least among the Malays in rural areas, it means "come over," similar to the index finger bent toward the body, a gesture which is used in certain Western countries, and should be used only for that purpose.
同样，挥手告别时，如果掌心向着挥手者自己（而不是向着要挥别的人），身处西班牙的英国游客可能会误以为这是请人回来的手势。	Similarly, a British traveller in Spain may mistake a wave goodbye involving the palm facing the waver (rather than the person being waved at) as a gesture to come back.
辅助语言是为了便于语言不相通的人群交流而创造的人工语言或构造语言。	Auxiliary languages are artificial or constructed languages created with the intent of facilitating communication between peoples who would otherwise have difficulty communicating.
他们不同于通用语。通用语是一种自然的或逐步形成的语言，由于各种原因成为其他语言使用者之间交流的主要手段。	They are separate from lingua francas, which are natural or organic languages that become dominant for one reason or another as means of communication between speakers of other languages.
在白天最热的时候，旅行者们可以体验到由水（或其他东西）所形成的错觉——海市蜃楼。	In the heat of the day, travelers can experience mirages that give the illusion of water (or other things).

据报道，人类感染禽流感的病例不到 一千例，但其中有一些病例是致命的。	Fewer than a thousand cases have ever been reported in humans, but some of them have been fatal.

在法国，传统上投票是一种没什么技术含量的体验：选民进到一个小隔间里，把一张预先印好的、表明了所选候选人的纸片装入信封中。	In France, voting has traditionally been a low-tech experience: voters isolate themselves in a booth, put a pre-printed sheet of paper indicating their candidate of choice into an envelope.

自 1988 年以来，投票箱就必须是透明的，这样选民和观察员才能看到投票开始时箱内没有信封，还能看到除了那些及时统计过、有权投票的选民以外，没有其他人向箱内投入信封。	Since 1988, ballot boxes must be transparent so that voters and observers can witness that no envelopes are present at the start of the vote and that no envelopes are added except those of the duly counted and authorized voters.

看守总理朱莉娅·吉拉德在2010年联邦大选竞选期间称，她认为在女王伊丽莎白二世退位后，澳大利亚应该成为共和国。	Caretaker Prime Minister Julia Gillard claimed during the campaign of the 2010 federal election that she believed Australia should become a republic at the end of Queen Elizabeth II's reign.
34% 的受访者一致表示，希望英国女王伊丽莎白二世成为澳大利亚的最后一任君主。	34 per cent of those in the poll share this view, wanting Queen Elizabeth II to be Australia's last monarch.
投票存在两极分化的情况，29% 的受访者认为澳大利亚应该尽快成立共和国，31% 的人则认为澳大利亚永远不应该成立共和国。	At the extremes of the poll, 29 per cent of those surveyed believe Australia should become a republic as soon as possible, while 31 per cent believe Australia should never become a republic.
这位奥运会金牌得主本应参加 100 米和 200 米自由泳和英联邦运动会的三项接力赛，但由于他的抱怨，他的健康状况一直受到质疑。	The Olympic gold medalist was due to swim in the 100m and 200m freestyle and in three relays at the Commonwealth Games, but due to his complaints his fitness has been in doubt.
他一直无法用药物来缓解疼痛，因为比赛禁止参赛者服用这些药物。	He has been unable to take the drugs needed to overcome his pain as they are banned from the Games.
中央密苏里大学 (University of Central Missouri) 的数学家、计算机科学教授柯蒂斯·库珀 (Curtis Cooper) 于 1 月 25 日发现了迄今为止最大的已知素数。	Curtis Cooper, a mathematician and computer science professor at the University of Central Missouri, has discovered the largest known prime number to date on January 25.
二月初，几个人用不同的硬件和软件验证了这一发现，并在周二宣布。	Several people verified the discovery using different hardware and software by the beginning of February and it was announced on Tuesday.
彗星可能是地球上的水和有机物的来源，这些有机物可以形成蛋白质并维持生命的存续。	Comets may possibly have been a source of water delivery to the earth along with organic matter that can form proteins and support life.
科学家希望了解自从彗星很久以前与地球相撞以来，行星是如何形成的，尤其是地球的形成方式。	Scientists hope to understand how planets form, especially how the Earth formed, since comets collided with the Earth long ago.
现年 53 岁的库莫（Cuomo）从今年年初开始担任州长，并于上个月签署了一项将同性婚姻合法化的法案。	Cuomo, 53, began his governorship earlier this year and signed a bill last month legalizing same-sex marriage.

据推测，他将在 2016 年参加总统竞选。	He is speculated to make a run for president in 2016.
美国联邦航空局 (FAA) 称，新一代航空运输系统 (NextGen) 可以使飞机缩短飞行航线，每年节省数百万加仑的燃料，并减少碳排放。	NextGen is a system the FAA claims would allow aircraft to fly shorter routes and save millions of gallons of fuel each year and cut carbon emissions.
它使用卫星技术，而不是老旧的地面雷达技术，使空中交通管制员能够更精确地定位飞机，并向飞行员提供更准确的信息。	It uses satellite-based technology as opposed to older ground-radar-based technology to allow air traffic controllers to pinpoint aircraft with greater precision and give pilots more accurate information.
没有增设额外的交通工具，地上火车在温布利 (Wembley) 也不停站，地上也没有停车场和停车换乘设施。	No extra transport is being put on and overground trains will not stop at Wembley, and car parking and park-and-ride facilities are unavailable at the ground.
由于担心缺乏交通工具，比赛可能会被迫在没有球队支持者的情况下闭门进行。	Fears of lack of transportation raised the possibility that the game would be forced to play behind closed doors without the team's supporters.
周四，一份发表于《科学》杂志的研究报告称，一种新的鸟类在厄瓜多尔加拉帕戈斯群岛形成。	A study published on Thursday in the journal Science reported on formation of a new bird species on the Ecuadorean Galápagos Islands.
来自美国普林斯顿大学和瑞典乌普萨拉大学的研究人员报告称，由于当地特有的达尔文雀中的勇地雀和外来的仙人掌大嘴地雀之间的繁殖，这个新物种只进化了两代，尽管人们认为这一过程需要更长的时间。	Researchers from Princeton University in the United States and Uppsala University in Sweden reported the new species evolved in just two generations, though this process had been believed to take much longer, due to breeding between an endemic Darwin finch, Geospiza fortes, and the immigrant cactus finch, Geospiza conirostris.
黄金可以加工成各种形状。可以卷曲成微小的形状。	Gold may be worked into all sorts of shapes. It can be rolled into tiny shapes.
它可以拉成细丝，用于缠绕和编结。也可以捶打或碾成片状。	It can be pulled into thin wire, which can be twisted and plaited. It can be hammered or rolled into sheets.
它可以做得很薄，粘在其他金属上，由于达到如此之薄，有时可以用于装饰被称为“彩饰手抄本”的书本里的手绘图画。	It can be made very thin, and stuck onto other metal. It can be made so thin that it was sometimes used to decorate the hand-painted pictures in books called "illuminated manuscripts".
这被称为化学物质的 pH 值。你可以使用红甘蓝汁制作指示剂。	This is called a chemical's pH. You can make an indicator using red cabbage juice.
卷心菜汁的颜色将根据化学物质的酸碱性发生变化。	The cabbage juice changes color depending on how acidic or basic (alkaline) the chemical is.
pH 值以被测化学品中的氢（pH 中的 H）离子数量表示。	The pH level is indicated by the amount of Hydrogen (the H in pH) ions in the tested chemical.
氢离子是失去了电子的质子（因为氢原子由一个质子和一个电子组成）。	Hydrogen ions are protons that had their electrons stripped off them (since Hydrogen atoms consist of one proton and one electron).
搅动两种干粉使其混合，然后用干净的湿手把它们揉成一个球。	Swirl the two dry powders together and then, with clean wet hands, squeeze them into a ball.
你手上的水分会与外层发生反应，这样会形成一层类似外壳的东西，感觉十分有趣。	The moisture on your hands will react with the outer layers, which will feel funny and form a sort of shell.
哈拉帕 (Harappa) 和摩亨佐-达罗 (Mohenjo-daro) 这两个城市几乎每家每户都有抽水马桶，这些马桶与精密的污水处理系统相连。	The cities of Harappa and Mohenjo-daro had a flush toilet in almost every house, attached to a sophisticated sewage system.
在希腊克里特岛和圣托里尼米诺斯城市的房屋中发现了污水系统的遗迹。	Remains of sewage systems have been found in the houses of the Minoan cities of Crete and Santorini in Greece.
古埃及、波斯和中国也有厕所。在罗马文明中，厕所有时是男女混合的公共浴室的一部分。	There were also toilets in ancient Egypt, Persia and China. In Roman civilization, toilets were sometimes part of public bath houses where men and women were together in mixed company.
你给远在千里之外的人打电话，就会用到卫星。	When you call someone who is thousands of miles away, you are using a satellite.
太空中的卫星接到电话后，几乎是立刻将其反射回去。	The satellite in space gets the call and then reflects it back down, almost instantly.
卫星是由火箭发射到太空的。科学家在太空中使用望远镜是因为地球的大气层让某些光线和视野产生扭曲。	The satellite was sent into space by a rocket. Scientists use telescopes in space because the Earth’s atmosphere distorts some of our light and view.
要把卫星或望远镜送入太空，需要一枚超过 100 英尺高的巨型火箭。	It takes a giant rocket over a 100 feet high to put a satellite or telescope in space.
车轮以不可思议的方式改变了世界。车轮对我们最大的贡献，是让我们的交通更加便捷。	The wheel has changed the world in incredible ways. The biggest thing that the wheel has done for us is given us much easier and faster transportation.
有了它，我们才有了火车、汽车和许多其他交通工具。	It has brought us the train, the car, and many other transportation devices.
它们的下方是更多中等大小的猫科动物，它们吃的是中等大小的猎物，从兔子、羚羊到鹿都会吃。	Under them are more medium sized cats that eat medium sized prey ranging from rabbits to antelopes and deer.
最终，有许多小型的猫科动物（包括散养的宠物猫），以昆虫、啮齿动物、蜥蜴和鸟类等数量多得多的小型猎物为食。	Finally, there are many small cats (including loose pet cats) that eat the far more numerous small prey like insects, rodents, lizards, and birds.
它们成功的秘诀是利基概念，每只猫都负责一项特殊的工作，防止它们与其他猫竞争。	The secret to their success is the concept of the niche, a special job each cat holds that keeps it from competing with others.
狮子是群居属性最明显的猫科动物，生活在称为狮群的大型群体中。	Lions are the most social cats, living in large groups called prides.
狮群由一到三只有亲属关系的成年雄性，以及可多达三十只的雌性和幼崽组成。	Prides are made up of one to three related adult males, along with as many as thirty females and cubs.
作为大家庭里的姐妹和女儿，雌性之间通常彼此关系密切。	The females are usually closely related to each other, being a large family of sisters and daughters.
狮群的行为与狼群或狗群非常类似。这些动物与狮子的行为惊人地相似（但与其他大型猫科动物不同），而且这些行为对它们的猎物来说也是非常致命的。	Lion prides act much like packs of wolves or dogs, animals surprisingly similar to lions (but not other big cats) in behavior, and also very deadly to their prey.
老虎是全能运动员，它会攀爬（虽然攀爬能力不是很强）、游泳、跳远，拉力能达到人类大力士的五倍。	A well rounded athlete, the tiger can climb (though not well), swim, leap great distances and pull with five times the force of a strong human.
老虎与狮、豹和美洲虎属于同一类型（豹属）。这四种大猫是仅有的会吼叫的猫科动物。	The tiger is in the same group (Genus Panthera) as lions, leopards, and jaguars. These four cats are the only ones who can roar.
老虎的咆哮不像狮子的咆哮那样深沉，而更像一句生气嘶吼的话语。	The tiger's roar is not like the full-voiced roar of a lion, but more like a sentence of snarly, shouted words.
豹猫喜欢吃小动物。如果条件允许，他们会捕捉猴子、蛇、啮齿动物和鸟类。豹猫的猎物几乎都比自身要小得多。	Ocelots like to eat small animals. They will catch monkeys, snakes, rodents and birds if they can. Almost all of the animals that the ocelot hunts are far smaller than it is.
科学家认为，美洲豹猫是通过气味和嗅探猎物在地面上的踪迹来跟踪和寻找要捕食的动物的。	Scientists think that ocelots follow and find animals to eat (prey) by smell, sniffing for where they've been on the ground.
它们的夜视能力很强，能在黑暗中看得很清楚，而且行动也很隐秘。豹猫的捕食方式是先融入周围环境，然后猛扑向猎物。	They can see very well in the dark with night vision, and move very stealthily, too. Ocelots hunt their prey by blending in with their surroundings then pouncing on their prey.
当一小群生物（一个小种群）与它们本来的主要种群分离时（比如它们跨过山脉和河流，或者它们到了一个新的岛屿以至于不可能轻易回去)，它们通常会发现自己所处的环境与之前不同。	When a small group of living things (a small population) gets separated from the main population that they came from (like if they move over a mountain range or a river, or if they move to a new island so that they can't easily move back) they will often find themselves in a different environment than they were in before.
这个新的环境有不同的资源和不同的竞争对手，所以新的种群将需要不同的特征或适应能力来成为一个强有力的竞争对手，而不是它们之前所需要的那些。	This new environment has different resources and different competitors, so the new population will need different features or adaptations to be a strong competitor than what they had needed before.
原来的种群根本没有改变，它们仍需要和以前一样适应环境。	The original population hasn't changed at all, they still need the same adaptations as before.
随着时间的推移，新的种群开始适应新的环境，它们开始变得与其他种群越来越不相似了。	Over time, as the new population begins to adapt to their new environment, they start to look less and less like the other population.
在历经数千甚至数百万年以后，这两个种群最终看上去会截然不同，以致于不能将两者称作同一物种。	Eventually, after thousands or even millions of years, the two populations will look so different that they can't be called the same species.
我们把这个过程称为“物种形成”，也就是新物种的形成。物种形成是进化的必然结果，也是进化中极为重要的一环。	We call this process speciation, which just means the formation of new species. Speciation is an unavoidable consequence and a very important part of evolution.
植物能制造人类吸入的氧气，吸收人类呼出的二氧化碳。	Plants make oxygen which humans breathe, and they take in carbon-dioxide which humans exhale (that is, breathe out).
植物通过光合作用从阳光中获取养分。它们还能提供荫凉。	Plants make their food from the sun by photosynthesis. They also provide shade.
我们用植物做房子，用植物做衣服。我们吃的大部分食物都是植物。没有植物，动物就不能生存。	We make our houses from plants and make clothes from plants. Most foods that we eat are plants. Without plants, animals could not survive.
沧龙是那个时代的顶级掠食者，除了同类它什么都不怕。	Mosasaurus was the apex predator of its time, so it feared nothing, except other mosasaurs.
它的长下颚上布满了 70 多颗剃刀般锋利的牙齿，上颚上还有一排。这意味着任何与它相遇的东西都无路可逃。	Its long jaws were studded with more than 70 razor-sharp teeth, along with an extra set in the roof of its mouth, meaning that there was no escape for anything that crossed its path.
它的舌头有可能是分叉的，对此我们尚不确定。它的食物包括海龟、大型鱼类、其他沧龙，甚至会吃人。	We don't know for sure, but it may have had a forked tongue. Its diet included turtles, large fish, other mosasaurs, and it may even have been a cannibal.
它会攻击任何进入水中的东西；即使像霸王龙之类的巨型恐龙也不是它的对手。	It also attacked anything that entered the water; even a giant dinosaur such as T. rex would be no match for it.
尽管罗马人的大部分食物是我们所常见的，但他们确实有一些奇怪或不寻常的宴会菜肴，包括野猪、孔雀、蜗牛和一种叫做榛睡鼠的啮齿动物	While most of their food would be familiar to us, Romans did have their share of strange or unusual feast items, including wild boar, peacock, snails, and a type of rodent called a dormouse
另一个不同之处在于，穷人和女人坐在椅子上吃饭，富人则喜欢聚在一起举行宴会，侧卧着吃饭。	Another difference was that while the poor people and the woman ate their food while sitting in chairs, the rich men liked to have banquets together where they would lounge on their sides while they ate their meals.
几个世纪后从美洲或亚洲传入欧洲的食物不可能出现在古罗马人的饮食当中。	Ancient Roman meals couldn't have included foods that came to Europe from America or from Asia in later centuries.
例如，他们没有玉米、西红柿、土豆和可可，也没有哪个古罗马人吃过火鸡。	For instance, they didn't have corn, nor tomatoes, nor potatoes, nor cocoa, and no ancient Roman ever tasted a turkey.
巴比伦人为他们每位神祇都建造了一座主殿，将其视为该神居所。	The Babylonians built each of their gods a primary temple that was considered the home of the god.
人们会把祭品献给神，牧师会通过仪式和节庆来满足神的需要。	People would bring sacrifices to the gods and the priests would try to attend to the needs of the gods through ceremonies and festivals.
每所神殿都有一处对外开放的庭院，以及一处只有祭司才能进入的内殿。	Each temple had an open temple courtyard and then an inner sanctuary that only the priests could enter.
有些特殊的塔呈金字塔形状，被称为金字形神塔，是作为庙宇的一部分而建造的。	Sometimes special pyramid shaped towers, called ziggurats, were built to be a part of the temples.
塔顶是上帝的特殊圣地。	The top of the tower was special sanctuary for the god.
在中东温暖的气候中，房子并不是多重要。	In the warm climate of the Middle East, the house was not so important.
希伯来家庭的生活大多是在户外度过的。	Most of the life of the Hebrew family happened in the open air.
女人们在院子里做饭；商店其实就是面向街道的开放柜台。他们用石头来建造房屋。	Women did the cooking in the yard; stores were just open counters looking into the street. Stone was used for building houses.
迦南没有大森林，所以木材非常昂贵。	There were no large forests in the land of Canaan, so wood was extremely expensive.
格陵兰岛人烟稀少。据北欧史诗萨迦记载，红胡子埃里克因犯谋杀罪被逐出冰岛，他向西航行，发现陆地，于是将其命名为格陵兰岛。	Greenland was settled sparsely. In the Norse sagas they say that Erik the Red was exiled from Iceland for murder, and when travelling further west, found Greenland and named it Greenland.
但不管他有没有发现，爱斯基摩人当时已经在那里生活了。	But regardless of his discovery, Eskimo tribes were already living there at the time.
虽然均隶属于“斯堪的纳维亚”，但丹麦、瑞典、挪威和冰岛的民众、国王、习俗和历史之间存在着许多差异。	Though each country was 'Scandinavian', there were many differences between the people, kings, customs and history of Denmark, Sweden, Norway and Iceland.
如果你看过电影《国家宝藏》，你可能会以为《独立宣言》背面会画着一份藏宝图。	If you have watched the movie National Treasure, you may think a treasure map was written on the back of the Declaration of Independence.
然而事实并非如此。虽然这份文件的背面写了一些东西，但并是不一份藏宝图。	However, that is not true. Although there is something written on the back of the document, it is not a treasure map.
《独立宣言》背面写着“Original Declaration of Independence dated 4th July 1776（《独立宣言》原件，1776 年 7 月 4 日）”的字样。文字写在文件底部，是倒过来的。	Written on the back of the Declaration of Independence were the words "Original Declaration of Independence dated 4th July 1776". The text appears on the bottom of the document, upside down.
虽然没有人能确定作者是谁，但这个大型羊皮纸文档（尺寸为 29¾ 英寸乘以 24½ 英寸）据称在刚写成的时候是卷起来存放的。	While no one knows for certain who wrote it, it is known that early in its life, the large parchment document (it measures 29¾ inches by 24½ inches) was rolled up for storage.
因此，很可能这个符号只是作为一个标签添加的。	So, it is likely that the notation was added simply as a label.
诺曼底登陆和随后的战斗解放了法国北部，但南部仍然没有解放。	The D-Day landings and the following battles had freed the north of France, but the south still wasn't free.
它由“维希”法国人统治。这些法国人在 1940 年与德国人达成了和平协议，不反抗侵略者，而是和他们合作。	It was ruled by the "Vichy" French. These were French people who had made peace with the Germans in 1940 and worked with the invaders instead of fighting them.
1940 年 8 月 15 日，盟军攻入法国南部，这次进攻被称为“龙骑兵行动”。	On 15 August 1940, the Allies invaded southern France, the invasion was called "Operation Dragoon".
仅仅两个星期，美国和自由法国的军队就解放了法国南部，并转向德国。	In just two weeks the Americans and Free French forces had liberated southern France and were turning towards Germany.
文明是一种由共同生活、合作工作的人群（社会）所共享的单一文化。	A civilization is a singular culture shared by a significant large group of people who live and work co-operatively, a society.
“文明”一词来自拉丁语“civilis”（意为“公民的”），与拉丁语"civis"（意为“公民”）及"civitas"（意为“城市”或“城邦”）都有关，这也以某种方式定义了社会的规模。	The word civilization comes from the Latin civilis, meaning civil, related to the Latin civis, meaning citizen, and civitas, meaning city or city-state, and that also somehow defines the size of the society.
城邦是民族的前身。文明型文化意味着知识的代代相传，文化的足迹萦绕留存，还有文化能够公平地传播。	City-states are the precursors of nations. A civilizational culture implies the passing on of knowledge across several generations, a lingering cultural footprint and fair dissemination.
少数民族文化常常没有留下相关的历史证据就消失无踪，而且不被当做是像样的文明。	Minor cultures often vanish without leaving relevant historic evidence and fail to be recognized as proper civilizations.
在独立战争期间，十三个州最初根据《联邦条例》组成了弱小的中央政府（国会是其唯一的组成部分）。	During the Revolutionary War, the thirteen states first formed a weak central government—with the Congress being its only component—under the Articles of Confederation.
国会没有征税的权力，而且因为没有国家行政部门或司法部门，国会只能依赖州政府执行所有法案，而州政府又经常不配合。	Congress lacked any power to impose taxes, and, because there was no national executive or judiciary, it relied on state authorities, who were often uncooperative, to enforce all its acts.
它也没有权力推翻各州之间的税法和关税。	It also had no authority to override tax laws and tariffs between states.
这些条款必须得到所有州的一致同意才能进行修改，而各州对待中央政府的态度十分轻慢，以至于其州立代表经常缺席。	The Articles required unanimous consent from all the states before they could be amended and states took the central government so lightly that their representatives were often absent.
意大利国家足球队和德国国家足球队都是世界上第二成功的球队，在 2006 年拿下了足球世界杯冠军。	Italy's national football, along with German national football team is the second most successful team in the world and were the FIFA World Cup champions in 2006.
流行的运动项目包括足球、篮球、排球、水球、击剑、橄榄球、自行车、冰球、轮滑曲棍球和一级方程式赛车。	Popular sports include football, basketball, volleyball, water-polo, fencing, rugby, cycling, ice hockey, roller hockey and F1 motor racing.
冬季运动在北部地区最受欢迎，意大利人会在那里参加国际比赛和奥运会比赛。	Winter sports are most popular in the Northern regions, with Italians competing in international games and Olympic events.
日本拥有近 7000 个岛屿（最大的是本州岛），这让日本成为了世界第七大岛国！	Japans holds nearly 7,000 islands (the biggest being Honshu), making Japan the 7th largest island in the world!
由于日本的岛屿群众多，日本从地质学角度上常被称为“列岛”	Due to the cluster/group of islands Japan has, Japan is often referred to, on a geographical stance, as an "archipelago"
西方对台湾的了解可以追溯到 15 世纪。当时路过的欧洲水手将该岛命名为“福尔摩沙岛”(Ilha Formosa)，意思是美丽的岛屿。	Taiwan beginning start way back in 15th century where European sailors passing by record the island’s name as Ilha Formosa, or beautiful island.
1624 年，荷兰东印度公司在台湾地区西南部建立基地，开始改变原住民的粮食生产方式，并雇佣华工在其水稻和蔗糖种植园工作。	In 1624,Dutch East India Company establishes a base in southwestern Taiwan, initiating a transformation in aboriginal grain production practices and employing Chinese laborers to work on its rice and sugar plantations.
1683 年，清朝（1644年 - 1912年）军队控制了台湾西部和北部沿海地区，1885 年，大清帝国宣布在台湾建省。	In 1683, Qing dynasty (1644-1912) forces take control of Taiwan’s western and northern coastal areas and declared Taiwan as a province of the Qing Empire in 1885.
1895 年，在甲午战争 (1894-1895 年) 中战败后，清政府签署了《马关条约》，将台湾的主权割让给日本，日本统治台湾直至 1945 年。	In 1895, after defeat in the First Sino-Japanese War (1894-1895), the Qing government signs the Treaty of Shimonoseki, by which it cedes sovereignty over Taiwan to Japan, which rules the island until 1945.
马丘比丘古城由三座主要建筑物组成，分别是拴日石 (Intihuatana)、太阳神庙和三窗之屋。	Machu Picchu consist of three main structures, namely Intihuatana, the Temple of the Sun, and the Room of the Three Windows.
为了让游客更好地了解建筑群的原貌，该建筑群边缘的大部分建筑都经过重建。	Most of the buildings on the edges of the complex have been rebuilt in order to give tourists a better idea of how they originally appeared.
到 1976 年，马丘比丘的百分之三十得到修复，修复工作一直持续到今天。	By 1976, thirty percent of Machu Picchu had been restored and restoration continues till today.
例如，世界上最常见的静态图像摄影格式是 35mm 格式，这是胶片电影时代末期占主导地位的电影尺寸。	For example, the most common still image photography format in the world is 35mm, which was the dominant film size at the close of the analog film era.
时至今日仍有生产，但更重要的是它的长宽比应用到了数码相机图像传感器的格式上。	It is still produced today, but more importantly its aspect ratio has been inherited by digital camera image sensor formats.
35 毫米格式的实际尺寸是 36 毫米宽，24 毫米高，这样格式其实有点令人困惑。	The 35mm format is actually, somewhat confusingly, 36mm in width by 24mm in height.
因此，这种格式的宽高比（除以 12 得到最简单的整数比）便是 3:2。	The aspect ratio of this format (dividing by twelve to obtain the simplest whole-number ratio) is therefore said to be 3:2.
许多常见格式（例如 APS 格式系列）都与这个长宽比相同或相当接近。	Many common formats (APS family of formats, for example) are equal to or closely approximate this aspect ratio.
经常被滥用和嘲笑的三分法，在创造动态时不失为一种简单的指导方法，还能让图像保持有序。	The much-abused and often-ridiculed rule of thirds is a simple guideline creating dynamism while keeping a measure of order in an image.
它指出，对主体来说最有效的位置是将图像垂直和水平分为三部分的线的交叉点（见示例）。	It states that the most effective place for the main subject is at the intersection of lines dividing the image into thirds vertically and horizontally (see example).
在欧洲历史上的这段时期，已然富有而强大起来的天主教会受到了密切监督。	During this period of European history, the Catholic Church, which had become rich and powerful, came under scrutiny.
尽管欧洲各国语言和习俗各不相同，但一千多年来，基督教把它们联系在了一起。	For over a thousand years the Christian religion had bound European states together despite differences in language and customs. I
从国王到平民，它遍布十方的力量影响着每一个人。	Its all-pervading power affected everyone from king to commoner.
基督教的主要信条之一是财富应该用来减轻痛苦和贫困，而教会的货币基金就是专门为此而设立的。	One of the main Christian tenets is that wealth should be used to alleviate suffering and poverty and that the monetary funds of the church are there specifically for that reason.
教会中央集权制在罗马存在了一千多年，这种权力和金钱的集中让许多人开始质疑，他们是否遵守了这一信条。	The central authority of the church had been in Rome for over a thousand years and this concentration of power and money led many to question whether this tenet was being met.
敌对行动爆发后不久，英国开始对德国实施海上封锁。	Soon after the outbreak of hostilities, Britain initiated a naval blockade of Germany.
他们切断了生死攸关的军事和民用物资供应。事实证明这一战略是有效的，尽管这样的封锁违反了在过去的两个世纪里，根据几项国际协定制定的已为大家普遍接受的国际法。	The strategy proved effective, cutting off vital military and civilian supplies, although this blockade violated generally accepted international law codified by several international agreements of the past two centuries.
英国在国际水域布雷，防止任何船只进入整片海域，甚至对中立国船只也构成威胁。	Britain mined international waters to prevent any ships from entering entire sections of ocean, causing danger to even neutral ships.
因为对这一战略的响应有限，德国期望其无限制潜艇战也能有类似的响应。	Since there was limited response to this tactic, Germany expected a similar response to its unrestricted submarine warfare.
在 20 世纪 20 年代，大多市民的主流态度是和平主义的、分离主义的。	During the 1920s, the prevailing attitudes of most citizens and nations was that of pacifism and isolation.
目睹第一次世界大战中的肆虐残暴后，各国都渴望避免重蹈覆辙。	After seeing the horrors and atrocities of war during World War I, nations desired to avoid such a situation again in the future.
1884 年，特斯拉搬到了美国，接受了纽约市爱迪生公司的一份工作。	In 1884, Tesla moved to the United States of America to accept a job with the Edison Company in New York City.
他在抵达美国时，身上带着 4 美分、一本诗集，还有一封查尔斯•巴舍勒（Charles Batchelor）（他前份工作的经理）写给托马斯•爱迪生（Thomas Edison）的推荐信。	He arrived in the US with 4 cents to his name, a book of poetry, and a letter of recommendation from Charles Batchelor (his manager in his previous job) to Thomas Edison.
中国古代的不同时期各有特点；中国的每个时期或每个执掌天下的家族都是一个特点鲜明的王朝。	Ancient China had a unique way of showing different time periods; each stage of China or each family that was in power was a distinctive dynasty.
同样，历朝历代更迭期间都是一段小国分立的不稳定时代。其中最有名的便是长达 60 年的三国时期，该时期处于汉晋两代的更迭之间。	Also between each dynasty was an unstable age of divided provinces. The best-known of these periods was the Three Kingdoms epoch taking place for 60 years between the Han and the Jin Dynasty.
在这些动乱时期，各路诸侯为争夺王位而发生激烈战争。	During these periods fierce warfare took place between many nobles fighting for the throne.
三国是中国古代历史上最血腥的时代之一。成千上万的人为了争夺西安豪华宫殿最高的权力而死去。	The Three Kingdoms was one of the bloodiest eras in Ancient China’s history thousands of people died fighting to sit in the highest seat in the grand palace at Xi’an.
还有许多社会和政治影响，例如度量单位的使用、从专制到共和制的转变、民族主义、相信国家不属于唯一的统治者而是属于人民。	There are a lot of social and political effects such as the use of metric system, a shift from absolutism to republicanism, nationalism and the belief the country belongs to the people not to one sole ruler.
此外，在革命之后，官职面向全体男性开放申请，这使得最有抱负、最成功之人有机会飞黄腾达。	Also after the Revolution occupations were open to all male applicants allowing the most ambitious and successful to succeed.
军队亦然，因为军衔的高低不再基于等级，而是基于才干。	Same goes for the military because instead of army rankings being based on class they were now based on cailaber.
法国大革命也鼓舞了许多其他国家被压迫的工人阶级，开始他们自己的革命。	The French Revolution also inspired many other repressed working class people of other country's to began their own revolutions.
穆罕默德对尘世生活之外的事十分感兴趣。他以前经常到“努尔”（光明）山上一个叫做”希拉“的山洞里去冥想。	Muhammad was deeply interested in matters beyond this mundane life. He used to frequent a cave that became known as “Hira‘” on the Mountain of “Noor” (light) for contemplation.
该洞穴本身，不仅经受住时间考验而保留下来，还为穆罕默德的灵性意向带来极其生动的形象。	he cave itself, which survived the times, gives a very vivid image of Muhammad’s spiritual inclinations.
该洞穴坐落在麦加 (Mecca) 北部的一座山顶上，与外界完全隔绝。	Resting on the top of one of the mountains north of Mecca, the cave is completely isolated from the rest of the world.
事实上，即使知道它的存在，也不容易找到。一旦进入洞穴，就完全与世隔绝了。	In fact, it is not easy to find at all even if one knew it existed. Once inside the cave, it is a total isolation.
除了清澈美丽的天空和周围的群山，什么也看不见。在洞穴中，几乎看不到也听不到外界的景象和声音。	Nothing can be seen other than the clear, beautiful sky above and the many surrounding mountains. Very little of this world can be seen or heard from inside the cave.
吉萨大金字塔是七大奇迹中唯一至今仍屹立不倒的建筑。	The Great Pyramid at Giza is the only one of the seven wonders that is still standing today.
大金字塔是埃及人在公元前三世纪的杰作，它是众多向已故法老表示敬意的大型金字塔的其中之一。	Built by the Egyptians in the third century BCE, the Great Pyramid is one of many large pyramid structures built to honor dead Pharaoh.
埃及死亡之谷的吉萨（Giza）高原（即“吉萨金字塔群”）包括多个金字塔（其中大金字塔是最大的）、几个小坟墓，几个寺庙和大狮身人面像。	The Giza Plateau, or "Giza Necropolis" in the Egyptian Valley of the Dead contains several pyramids (of which the great pyramid is the largest), several small tombs, several temples, and the great Sphinx.
大金字塔是为纪念胡夫法老而建造的，并为纪念胡夫的妻子和家庭成员建造了多座较小的金字塔、坟墓和庙宇。	The great pyramid was created to honor the Pharaoh Khufu, and many of the smaller pyramids, tombs, and temples were built to honor Khufu's wives and family members.
“上弓”符号像字母 V，“下弓”符号像是钉书钉或是缺少了底边的正方形。	The "up bow" mark looks like a V and the "down bow mark" like a staple or a square missing its bottom side.
向上指的是从顶端开始推弓，向下指的是从弓根处（也就是手握弓的地方）开始拉弓。	Up means you should start at the tip and push the bow, and down means you should start at the frog (which is where your hand is holding the bow) and pull the bow.
上弓通常会发出更加柔和的声音，而下弓则会发出更强烈、更为坚定的声响。	An up-bow usually generates a softer sound, while a down-bow is stronger and more assertive.
